</ol> \n   <hr> \n    <h2>What are the best PC gaming headsets?</h2> \n    <p>When indulging in PC gaming, it's easy to get sucked into the hardware that makes up your rig and push for ultimate graphics and frame rates. However, the sound shouldn't ever be overlooked. Not only is it one of the most immersive aspects of a game, but in titles like competitive shooters, being able to pinpoint where sounds are coming from can be the difference between winning and losing. For most, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/SteelSeries-Arctis-GameDAC-Headset-playstation-4/dp/B079YBKTRN?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU40843YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">SteelSeries Arctis Pro + GameDAC</a> ticks all the boxes while being extremely comfortable, while the similar <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/SteelSeries-Arctis-Wireless-Gaming-Headset-Console/dp/B086M4DQ7R?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU40843YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Arctis 1</a> is a solid alternative for folks looking to spend less and also have a console-ready headset. Then if you're into competitive gaming, particularly first-person shooters, something like the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU40843YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Frazer-blackshark-v2-multi-platform-wired-esports-headset-with-usb-sound-card-black%252F6417115.p%253FskuId%253D6417115&amp;token=VXySKmR_\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Razer BlackShark V2</a> was entirely designed for you. Meanwhile, gamers shopping on a tight budget can still get a truly excellent headset with the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Plugable-Performance-Retractable-Microphone-Playstation/dp/B07P71F7XR/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU40843YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Plugable Performance Onyx HS53</a>.</p> \n    <p>Here's our breakdown of what the best PC gaming headset you can buy is, so take a look and see which best fits your requirements and your budget.</p> \n    <p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/SteelSeries-Arctis-GameDAC-Headset-playstation-4/dp/B079YBKTRN?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU40843YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-pc-gaming-headsets\" title=\"Best PC Gaming Headset 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/steelseries-arctis-pro-sehero-1.jpg\" /></a></p> \n    <h2 id=\"arctispro\">1. you should consider. The quality of the audio experience is too easy to overlook, but if your audio is bad, then you're just not going to enjoy yourself as much. Regardless of your budget, spending on the wrong headset for you is a waste.</p> \n     <p>The first thing you should consider is just what type of PC gaming you do most. If you're a regular competitive shooter player, for example, you're going to have different preferences compared to someone who plays sports games. The former would look for good directional audio capabilities, while the latter can get away without a lot of it.</p> \n     <p>It's also worth considering how you want to connect to your PC. Wired has many advantages over wireless, not least that you don't have to worry about battery life. However, it's also not as convenient as having no cables dangling from your head, especially if you don't sit incredibly close to your PC. If you also want to play on a console as well as PC, wired becomes a much easier solution to live with.</p> \n     <p>There's also the little matter of the microphone. While this doesn't directly benefit your experience, your gaming buddies will thank you a whole lot if your voice is loud enough, clear, and free of background noise. Harmony among your team is well worth it! There's also the matter of a detachable microphone if you, for example, plan to use your headset as a regular pair of headphones. Retractable would be a bare minimum in this case, but detachable is best.</p> \n     <hr> \n      <p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/HyperX-Cloud-Alpha-Leatherette-HX-HSCAS-BK/dp/B081D8TPZZ?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU40843YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-pc-gaming-headsets\" title=\"Best PC Gaming Headset 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/hyper-x-cloud-alpha-blackout-sehero-1.jpg\" /></a></p> \n      <h2 id=\"hyperx\">2. It's an exceptionally comfortable headset with a great microphone, a subtle design that means you can easily get away using it as a pair of headphones outdoors without feeling silly as well as virtual surround sound for an immersive experience.</p> \n      <p><strong>Speakers:</strong> 50mm neodymium | <strong>Frequency response:</strong> 13Hz – 27,000Hz | <strong>Compatibility:</strong> USB, 3.5mm | <strong>Impedance:</strong> 65 ohms | <strong>Features:</strong> Detachable mic, braided cable with in-line remote, dual-chamber audio set up</p> \n      <table class=\"alternating\"> \n       <thead> \n        <tr> \n         <th>Manufacturer</th> \n         <th>Headset</th> \n         <th>Vendor</th> \n        </tr> \n       </thead> \n       <tbody> \n        <tr> \n         <td><strong>Hyper X</strong></td> \n         <td><strong>Cloud Alpha S Blackout</strong></td> \n         <td><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU40843YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fhyperx-cloud-alpha-s-wired-7-1-surround-sound-gaming-headset-for-pc-with-chat-mixer-and-adjustable-bass-blackout%252F6407589.p%253FskuId%253D6407589&amp;token=tHm9FRfF\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop no-alt-cta norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$130 at Best Buy</a></td> \n        </tr> \n       </tbody> \n      </table> \n      <h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3> \n      <ul> \n       <li>7.1 virtual surround, remote/mixer</li> \n       <li>Stunning sound reproduction</li> \n       <li>Great microphone</li> \n       <li>Signature HyperX comfort</li> \n       <li>High-quality construction, new black color</li> \n      </ul> \n      <h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3> \n      <ul> \n       <li>The cord is too long for the remote</li> \n       <li>Some optional customization software would be nice</li> \n      </ul> \n      <p>HyperX makes some compelling gaming headsets. They're among the best in the business, and <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-hyperx-headsets\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">we've recommended plenty</a>. The <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/hyperx-cloud-alpha-s-blackout-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">HyperX Cloud Alpha S Blackout</a> is almost the same as the lower-priced Cloud Alpha, but with the addition of a mixer remote that delivers <strong>7.1 surround sound</strong> and a new \"Blackout\" color scheme. It costs a little more, but it's worth it.</p> \n      <p>The Cloud Alpha S Blackout sports a sturdy aluminum frame with replaceable ear cups, and you can choose between leatherette or foam. Regardless of which you opt for, both options are <strong>comfortable for even longer gaming sessions</strong>. Utilizing dual 50mm drivers and HyperX's \"dual-chamber\" design, you'll be able to enjoy music and in-game effects without the headset muddying the highs and lows.</p> \n      <p>The <strong>bass is pretty punchy</strong>, too, and you can control it by using physical switches on each earcup to set your desired level. Overall, the audio quality, especially given this mid-tier price for gaming headsets, is amazing. The microphone is pretty good too, which is handy when you plan on communicating with friends and guildmates.</p> \n      <p>What you may find annoying with the Blackout is the rather long cable. Usually, this isn't an issue, but this cable is <em>long</em>. SteelSeries Arctis 1 Wireless Xbox: <em>A versatile headset for both PC and console gaming</em></h2> \n           <p><strong>Bottom line:</strong> Getting an excellent wireless headset that can handle both PC and console with ease isn't as straightforward as it could be, and the Arctis 1 fits the bill. Not only does it sound great with similar drivers to the Arctis Pro, and have good battery life, it's got dependable cross-platform support.</p> \n           <p><strong>Speakers:</strong> 40mm | <strong>Frequency response:</strong> 20–20,000 Hz | <strong>Compatibility:</strong> Wireless (Xbox and PC), 3.5mm | <strong>Impedance:</strong> 32 ohms</p> \n           <table class=\"alternating\"> class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3> \n           <ul> \n            <li>Superb comfort</li> \n            <li>Great design</li> \n            <li>20-hour battery life</li> \n            <li>Same drivers as Arctis Pro line</li> \n            <li>True cross-platform support</li> \n           </ul> \n           <h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3> \n           <ul> \n            <li>Only one dongle</li> \n            <li>Microphone is average at best</li> \n            <li>Micro USB port for charging</li> \n           </ul> \n           <p>SteelSeries makes great headsets, and the company brought lossless 2.4GHz wireless features to the budget-friendly Arctis 1 range. To make this headset even more awesome, SteelSeries threw in <strong>Xbox Wireless compatibility</strong>, making this one versatile gaming headset. Whether you game on PC, Xbox, PlayStation, or even Switch, this will be a fine companion.</p> \n           <p>As we discovered in our <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/steelseries-arctis-1-xbox-edition-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">SteelSeries Arctis 1 Wireless Xbox review</a>, the headset does require a dongle to connect to consoles. However, the Xbox version does have built-in support for Microsoft's Xbox Wireless protocols. However, this does all mean you get excellent audio without being tethered to one single device.</p> \n           <p>If you don't want to use the dongle, there's a 3.5mm cable that can be used. As well as this cable, SteelSeries includes a <strong>USB-A to USB-C converter</strong> for the dongle, and USB-A to micro USB cable to charge the headset itself. For the design, it's very much an Arctis headset. The only significant difference between the Arctis 1 and other headsets from SteelSeries is the lack of a ski-band.</p> \n           <p>This is a bit of a bummer, but understandable given the price of the Arctis 1. It's still a <strong>comfortable headset</strong> to use, just not as comfy as, say, the Arctis Pro. There's also the microphone, which is a little underwhelming, but so long as you're not planning to start streaming, you should be good to go.</p> \n           <div class=\"rows left collection\"> \n            <h3 class=\"product reco-block\">SteelSeries Arctis 1 Xbox</h3> \n            <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-pc-gaming-headsets\" title=\"Best PC Gaming Headset 2020\" gaming headsets?</h2> \n            <p>Shopping for the best PC gaming headset will involve checking out a host of products on the market today from brands you've heard of and brands you haven't, including those not mentioned here. Gaming is big business, and so every company that can naturally wants to be in on the action. So while these are the best, there's still a lot of alternatives out there.</p> \n            <p>More specifically, there's an increasing choice when it comes to budget headsets for both PC and console, like shopping for the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-xbox-gaming-headsets-under-100\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Best Xbox Gaming Headsets Under $100</a> or just the flat out <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-xbox-one-headsets\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best Xbox One headset</a> to use alongside your PC escapades.</p> \n            <hr> \n             <h2>How to choose the right PC gaming headset</h2> \n             <p>Choosing a headset is a personal decision that should take into account what you want from a pair of cups. Do you want a wireless option, or is wireless fine for you? Do you need the absolute best in sound quality for competitive play (that way, you can hear all those footsteps and which direction they might be coming from), or are you alright with a budget headset with solid sound for general play?</p> \n             <p>There's plenty more to factor in, too, even if you limit your search to gaming headsets alone. This is why we put together this collection of headsets from top vendors. There are some high-end, premium options, as well as more affordable and budget orientated cups. You can't go wrong by choosing one of our recommendations. We've tried them all and enjoyed each experience.</p> \n             <p>The final decision should come down to a combination of the type of games you want to play, whether you're looking for things like console support as well or want to go wireless, and yes, your budget. No matter how good a headset is, if it's over what you want to pay, then it's not a good headset for you.</p> \n             <h2>What to look for in a new PC gaming headset</h2> \n             <p>Use this handy checklist to cover off the key features you should consider when you're shopping for a new headset.</p> \n             <ul class=\"col2\"> \n              <li>Budget</li> \n              <li>Directional audio / Virtual surround sound</li> \n              <li>Gaming only or media use</li> \n              <li>Just PC or console also</li> \n              <li>Wired or wireless</li> \n              <li>Microphone quality</li> \n              <li>Detachable microphone</li> \n              <li>Battery life on wireless headsets</li> \n             </ul> \n             <h2 class=\"no-amazon\">Credits — The team that worked on this guide</h2> \n             <p class=\"credit\"><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-pc-gaming-headsets\" title=\"Best PC Gaming Headset 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2018/08/richard-avatar.jpg\" /></a></p> \n             <p class=\"end\"><strong>Richard Devine</strong> Richard Devine is an Editor at Windows Central. classic.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Minecraft</a> is hardly known for having cutting edge graphics. Instead, it focuses on addictive gameplay lined with bewilderingly deep mechanics. However, people have long been asking for Minecraft to be blessed with something more thorough than a regular texture pack. After the planned 'Super Duper Graphics Pack' for the Xbox One X was <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-super-duper-graphics-pack-canceled-didnt-perform-well-across-devices\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">unfortunately canceled</a> due to disappointing performance, it really looked like we were going to be left without any sort of visual upgrade for Minecraft.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing-beta\" title=\"\" class=\"cta large norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Related: How to play the Minecraft with RTX beta</a></p> \n   <p>Much to our surprise, what was previously a collection of rumors or projects by mad computer wizards in their basements was officially revealed just a week later: ray tracing is coming to Minecraft. Here's everything you need to know about Minecraft with RTX:</p> \n   <!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <h3 class=\"category reco-block\">A gaming masterpiece</h3> \n   <h4 class=\"product\">Minecraft</h4> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2019/11/minecraft-reco-image.jpg?itok=7_ELnb8r\" /></a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU75570YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fp%252Fminecraft-for-windows-10-master-collection%252F9pbpd1ftzlcv%253Factivetab%253Dpivot%25253Aoverviewtab&amp;token=QYEtuzBr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$50 at Microsoft (Windows 10 Master Collection)</a> <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU75570YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fp%252Fminecraft-for-windows-10-starter-collection%252F9n4km90ctzt6%253Factivetab%253Dpivot%25253Aoverviewtab&amp;token=kGAwxLHJ\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$30 at Microsoft (Windows 10 Starter Collection)</a></p> \n   <p class=\"subtitle\">Available everywhere you play.</p> \n   <p class=\"end\">Minecraft is an inarguable and complete success. It has sold copies in the hundreds of millions, has a huge following of dedicated players, and lets you unlock your every creative desire. It's also available on every platform imaginable, including Xbox One, Windows 10, Playstation 4, and Nintendo Switch. Play with anyone, and play anywhere.</p> \n   <!-- END RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <!--sectionbreak:article-nav-menu narrow no-amazon mobile-always--> \n   <h3>Jump to:</h3> \n   <ul class=\"jumplist col2\"> </ul> \n   <!--sectionbreak--> \n   <h2 id=\"rtx\">What is <em>Minecraft with RTX?</em></h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-01.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Minecraft with RTX isn't an entirely separate product, it's just a new branch of Minecraft building on the Bedrock Edition, and is currently only available on Windows 10 PC's with compatible NVIDIA hardware. Minecraft with RTX seeks to bring all the visual prowress of ray tracing, powered by NVIDIA's 20-series RTX GPU's, to everyone's favorite creative survival game. Right now, Minecraft with RTX is only available as a <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing-beta\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">beta, which anyone can sign up for</a>, but should eventually be available to anyone who has the hardware to run it.</p> \n   <p>According to Mojang Studios and NVIDIA, there's a chance for Minecraft with RTX to expand beyond Windows 10 PC's as well, including possibly next-gen consoles like the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/xbox-series-x\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Xbox Series X</a>.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"news\">What are the <em>latest news and leaks</em> for Minecraft with RTX?</h2> \n   <h3 class=\"aside\">Minecraft with RTX gets first major update in months, adds the Nether Update—September 3, 2020</h3> \n   <p class=\"end\">After months of practically silence, <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/new-minecraft-rtx-beta-1163052-brings-ray-tracing-nether-update\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Minecraft with RTX is getting a major update</a> that brings the beta to the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-nether-update\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">1.16 Nether Update</a> release, and adds new maps to try out in the Minecraft Marketplace. This is also known as Beta Pack #3.</p> \n   <h3 class=\"aside\">Mojang Studios releases the Beta Pack #2 update for Minecraft with RTX—May 15, 2020</h3> \n   <p class=\"end\">The beta for Minecraft with RTX has received its first major update, with Beta Pack #2 <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-adds-new-worlds-and-effects-beta-windows-10\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">now being released</a>. There are five new maps to check out, with more gameplay, effects, and textures taking advantage of NVIDIA's ray tracing technology. Exciting stuff, indeed, and shows the progress of improvements in Minecraft with RTX.</p> \n   <h3 class=\"aside\">The Minecraft with RTX beta has been confirmed for an April 16, 2020 release—April 14, 2020</h3> \n   <p class=\"end\">It's finally here! RTX ray tracing is coming to <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/first-beta-build-minecraft-ray-tracing-april-16\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Minecraft in beta-form on April 16, 2020</a>, through the Xbox Insider Hub on Windows 10. You'll have to be involved in the Xbox Insider program, and you'll need an NVIDIA RTX 2060 GPU or greater to run it. This isn't the full release, but it means anyone with the hardware can now get their hands on the technology and take it for a test drive. We have all the details <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing-beta\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">for how to play the Minecraft with RTX beta</a>.</p> \n   <h3 class=\"aside\">Minecraft with RTX is \"coming soon,\" according to NVIDIA—March 31, 2020</h3> \n   <p class=\"end\">We still don't have an official confirmation or a definitive date, but according to NVIDIA, <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/nvidia-releases-more-information-ray-tracing-minecraft-says-its-coming-soon\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">ray tracing for Minecraft is \"coming \"soon\"</a>. Hopefully, it won't be too much longer now.</p> \n   <h3 class=\"aside\">NVIDIA releases new videos and guides for Minecraft with RTX—March 31, 2020</h3> \n   <p class=\"end\">NVIDIA has released new videos and guides diving into the tech behind ray tracing in Minecraft, and there's some pretty impressive information here. The videos go over various aspects of Minecraft with RTX, and how creators can get started creating their own worlds and designs with ray tracing turned on. All of this can be found on <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D44270%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU75570YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.nvidia.com%252Fen-us%252Fgeforce%252Fnews%252Fminecraft-with-rtx-coming-soon-screenshots-and-guides%252F%253Fncid%253Dafm-chs-44270%2526ranMID%253D44270%2526ranEAID%253DkXQk6%25252AivFEQ%2526ranSiteID%253DkXQk6.ivFEQ-fOc00tYdazSjNcfImmsorA&amp;token=mK4q_d6s\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA's website</a>, and is a pretty useful resource to have.</p> \n   <h3 class=\"aside\">Microsoft offers a comment on the Xbox Series X running Minecraft with RTX demo—March 17, 2020</h3> \n   <p class=\"end\">We reached out for Microsoft to comment on the demo, and they offered us this statement: <em>\"Austin Evans saw a technical demonstration designed to show off the capabilities of hardware-accelerated DirectX Raytracing on Xbox Series X. It is not a product announcement.\"</em> While not a flat out denial that it could come in the future, the Evans demo isn't indicative of any upcoming announcement.</p> \n   <h3 class=\"aside\">Minecraft with RTX was teased in a demo running on the Xbox Series X—March 16, 2020</h3> \n   <p class=\"end\">Microsoft has openly <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-teases-ray-tracing-support-minecraft-xbox-series-x\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">teased ray tracing support</a> for Minecraft on the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/xbox-series-x\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Xbox Series X.</a> While nothing has been confirmed, Microsoft did use ray tracing in Minecraft as a technical demo for the technology, while discussing the deep-founded support the Series X will have for ray tracing. The support may not be entirely exclusive to NVIDIA graphics cards since AMD is the company powering the next-gen console.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"trailers\">Where can I <em>watch the trailers</em> for Minecraft with RTX?</h2> \n   <p>We've collected all the official trailers for Minecraft with RTX into one place, that way you can watch them whenever you want. <h2 id=\"reveal\">When was <em>Minecraft with RTX revealed</em>?</h2> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/91kxRGeg9wQ?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-91kxrgeg9wq\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>On August 19, 2019, NVIDIA released a reveal trailer for RTX ray tracing in Minecraft—and it's seriously gorgeous. It utilizes DXR and DirectX 12 (Microsoft's industry standards for ray tracing and other gaming technologies) so that Minecraft can, for the first time, accurately portray lighting, shadows, shaders, textures, and even reflections with perfect accuracy, all in real-time.</p> \n   <p>The announcement was a little sudden and unexpected but welcomed by Minecraft's passionate community. With ray tracing, Minecraft takes realism to a whole new level without losing anything (even mod support!).</p> \n   <p>The reveal trailer above really says it all, and it's definitely worth a watch.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"what\">What can <em>ray tracing do</em> for Minecraft with RTX?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-02.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Before ray tracing was introduced to the gaming world, particle effects and lighting were simulated and artificial, and therefore lacked a dynamic feel. That isn't to say games still couldn't be breathtakingly beautiful without ray tracing, but it did mean there was always a limit that no amount of coding could overcome. With ray tracing, games can track the paths of light through an environment dynamically and in real-time, meaning things like reflections, shading, and patterns of light could look more life-like and authentic.</p> \n   <p>For most games, this leads to a subtle effect that is incredibly striking when noticed but doesn't necessarily alter the entire feel of a scene. A lot of games are already designed to be realistic, and clever tricks and techniques mean modern \"AAA\" games can look better than real life with enough power behind them.</p> \n   <p>Minecraft, of course, has never been built to look realistic or even conventionally beautiful. Minecraft's graphics are meant to be straightforward, flexible, and simple enough that even lower-end hardware can handle them with aplomb. They're not something you forget, but they certainly don't take your breath away.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing-hands\" title=\"\" class=\"cta large norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Hands-on: Minecraft with RTX upgrades got me addicted to ray tracing</a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-03.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <blockquote class=\"big pull right\"> \n    <p>Ray tracing completely alters Minecraft, leading to a very different game.</p> \n   </blockquote> \n   <p>In Minecraft with RTX, ray tracing is far more dramatic. Instead of barely-noticeable lighting effects and reflections, ray tracing completely alters Minecraft at its core, leading to a very different feeling game. Minecraft with RTX goes from simple and unassuming graphics to blowing your mind every time you turn a corner. Every screenshot of Minecraft with RTX and ray tracing turned on feels like a talented fan's custom render rather than something that can actually be real. And <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D44270%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU75570YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.nvidia.com%252Fen-us%252Fgeforce%252Fnews%252Fminecraft-rtx-trailer-screenshots-partnership%252F&amp;token=k6vsziOg\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA's site</a> is full of side-by-side comparisons to alleviate your cravings.</p> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/-_4QaWbntUQ?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;start=0\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-4qawbntuq\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>NVIDIA and Minecraft haven't been shy about showing the tech off either. Last November, and even earlier this year, they invited a few lucky (and very skilled) Minecraft players to experience Minecraft with RTX, and see what they could build. The result was a showcase of some impressive designs that shows ray tracing even shifts the way you have to think when building in Minecraft. Much like in real life, details become even more critical, with simple things like natural light changing how a scene looks and feels. Updated textures and shading make different blocks give off new emotions and ambiances.</p> \n   <p>And then, NVIDIA turned around and gave players access to these carefully designed worlds, letting anyone with the necessary hardware explore Minecraft with ray tracing turned on. The results are appropriately stunning, if unpolished and rough around the edges in early beta.</p> \n   <p>What can ray tracing do for Minecraft? The answer is simple: a lot. The reason behind the answer? Not quite as simple.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"how\">How does <em>ray tracing work</em> in Minecraft with RTX?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-04.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Ray tracing in Minecraft isn't as simple as flipping a switch (at least, not until it's finished) and accomplishes a lot more than a simple shader pack. Shader packs use pre-existing code and build on top of it, trying to alter the appearance of Minecraft with a rendered layer on top of everything. Ray tracing will be built into the foundation of Minecraft with RTX and will work from the inside out to dynamically alter all of Minecraft. This means better visual fidelity, superior performance, and a subtle shift from pre-generated guesswork to accurate and real-time tracking of lighting and texture information. Those intimately familiar with shader packs may not see as dramatic a shift, but the difference is there.</p> \n   <p>The effect is most obvious when you're in motion. Static screenshots do a fair job of displaying the tech's more alluring qualities, but those familiar with shaders will claim they've seen it before. When you're in the game, the ability for ray tracing to alter scenes in real-time dynamically is powerful, and clear to see.</p> \n   <p>So how does all of this work?</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-05.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Getting the technology up and running in Minecraft with RTX comes down to one main thing: NVIDIA's RTX-capable graphics cards—like those in our roundup of <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best graphics cards</a>—and Mojang's Render Dragon engine. Ray tracing is just coming to the Windows 10 version of Minecraft: Bedrock Edition at first because only the Render Dragon engine present in Bedrock supports such technologies like DXR ray tracing through Microsoft's DirectX 12, which don't exist in Java right now.</p> \n   <blockquote class=\"big pull left\"> \n    <p>The Render Dragon engine is more modern, flexible, and powerful than the old Minecraft engine.</p> \n   </blockquote> \n   <p>When Mojang set out to build the Bedrock Edition, they needed an engine that could span platforms, no matter the architecture of the processor (like the difference between a phone and a desktop computer), the power available, or the technologies being used. The Render Dragon can support a ton of awesome features, which is evident by looking at the AR magic of <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-earth/home\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Minecraft Earth</a> and its new lighting techniques. At the end of the day, the Render Dragon engine in Minecraft: Bedrock Edition is more modern, flexible, and powerful than the old engine in Minecraft: Java Edition. It runs great if you're on a low-end Android phone or a high-end gaming PC.</p> \n   <p>It also supports DirectX 12 and Microsoft's industry-standard ray tracing APIs. So, with some work, the Render Dragon engine can tap directly into NVIDIA's powerful RTX graphics cores to deliver real-time hardware-accelerated ray tracing.</p> \n   <p>A Windows 10 PC + a powerful NVIDIA GPU + Minecraft: Bedrock Edition = a gorgeous and dynamic experience.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"beta\">How can I <em>play the beta</em> for Minecraft with RTX?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-06.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Minecraft with RTX is a pretty big deal, and if you have the setup it's understandable that you'd want to jump in and check out what all the fuss is about. Fortunately, we've already covered everything players need to try out Minecraft with RTX, and while there are a few steps involved (and potential upgrades for your computer), it's relatively straightforward to get ray tracing turned on in Minecraft. To play the beta for Minecraft with RTX, you'll need to:</p> \n   <ul> \n    <li><strong>Check to make sure your computer can handle it.</strong> Minecraft with RTX is more resource-hungry than normal Minecraft, but more than that it requires very specific hardware to run. Check the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-requirements\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">minimum and recommended requirements for Minecraft with RTX</a> to ensure your computer can make the cut.</li> \n    <li><strong>Follow these steps to enroll and receive the update.</strong> The Minecraft with RTX beta runs through the Xbox Insider Hub, and you may need to install some specific Game Ready drivers from NVIDIA as well. <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing-beta\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Follow these steps to play the Minecraft with RTX beta</a>, and you should be good to go.</li> \n   </ul> \n   <h2 id=\"release\">When is the <em>release date</em> for Minecraft with RTX?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-07.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>If you came here seeking a definitive day that you can mark on your calendars, you might walk away disappointed. Mojang and NVIDIA haven't given an exact date for the release of Minecraft with RTX, only that it's coming \"within the next year.\" Considering that ray tracing was officially announced in mid-August 2019, this would put Minecraft with RTX up for a Summer 2020 release date, although that obviously didn't happen. We did get the beta for Minecraft with RTX within that first year, so it's possible that's what NVIDIA and Mojang Studios were referring to. For anything regarding a full release, we'll have to wait for more information.</p> \n   <p>There is one bright side though: NVIDIA and Mojang have already announced that this update will be completely free. If you have the setup for it, you'll be able to reap the benefits of RTX ray tracing the moment it comes out. Yay! Mojang also confirmed that while ray tracing will launch exclusively on Windows 10 PCs, it will eventually come to other platforms that also support the technology.</p> \n   <p>Additionally, the Render Dragon engine allows Minecraft to do platform-specific updates to improve graphics or performance depending on the device. Even if your device can't handle ray tracing, you may still notice improvements over time.</p> \n   <p>There's more information to be found on <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D44270%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU75570YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.nvidia.com%252Fen-us%252Fgeforce%252Fnews%252Fminecraft-ray-tracing-your-questions-answered%252F&amp;token=ltULgeN7\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA's Q&amp;A post</a> if you want to take a peek.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"xbox\">Will the <em>Xbox Series X</em> get Minecraft with RTX?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/03/xbox-series-x-with-controller.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>A question on everyone's mind since the moment the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/xbox-series-x\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Xbox Series X</a> was revealed was \"Will Minecraft get ray tracing support?\" After all, up until this point ray tracing had been all NVIDIA, with AMD claiming support was coming <em>in the future</em>, but with no definitive information. With ray tracing being touted as a next-gen feature in Microsoft's newest console, which runs on AMD hardware, things were starting to get exciting. But will Minecraft, a very public partner with NVIDIA on ray tracing technology, recieve the same treatment on Xbox Series X?</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-xbox-series-x\" title=\"\" class=\"cta large norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Related: Everything you need to know about Minecraft on the Xbox Series X</a></p> \n   <p>The answer is a resounding <em>probably</em>. Microsoft demoed ray tracing on an Xbox Series X using Minecraft, but later reached out to us and commented that the demonstration was technical only, and not indicative of a product announcement. While this doesn't officially confirm Minecraft with RTX on the Xbox Series X, the fact that it <em>is</em> running in limited fashion makes us extremely hopeful that it is, in fact, coming. Minecraft is one of Microsoft's biggest games, and it only makes sense to make sure Minecraft takes full advantage of the Xbox Series X and it's seriously impressive hardware.</p> \n   <p>However, even if we can safely assume that Minecraft will receive the next-gen treatment on Xbox Series X, complete with ray tracing, we have no way of knowing when it'll happen. Ray tracing with NVIDIA cards on Windows 10 is still very early on, with missing textures, unstable performance, and general bugs and glitches. There's little reason to believe that ray tracing will be farther along on AMD hardware, which has much less real-world experience running ray tracing in video games.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-rtx-ray-tracing\" title=\"Minecraft with RTX: Ray tracing, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/minecraft-rtx-screenshot-08.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>On that note, it's also possible it won't be considered \"Minecraft with RTX\" on next-gen consoles like the Xbox Series X, just because RTX is strictly an NVIDIA feature, even if ray tracing technically isn't. So while AMD's newest hardware is ray tracing capable, AMD can't claim to be using NVIDIA's RTX cores in their GPU's.</p> \n   <p>I would expect ray tracing and other next-gen specific features to come to <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/minecraft-xbox-series-x\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Minecraft on Xbox Series X</a> in a future update, after launch, through Xbox's <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/xbox-series-x-smart-delivery\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Smart Delivery</a>. Microsoft will want to make sure that the experience is a flawless showcase of their new hardware, so it'll probably need a little extra time in the oven. That's alright, because Minecraft itself should be on Xbox Series X day one, thanks to backwards compatibility, and can still benefit from the speed and power of Xbox Series X in other ways.</p> \n   <p>As for ray tracing, or other visual and performance upgrades, we might have to wait just a little bit longer.</p> \n   <h2>Ray tracing and Minecraft—a perfect fit</h2> \n   <p>Combining the timeless joy of Minecraft with RTX and the breathtaking graphics of modern games seems like a no-brainer, and ray tracing will make that a reality. As you can see from pretty much every example of the tech in Minecraft, it's an impressive transition that makes me a little incredulous, but excited nonetheless. Ray tracing is a big shift for Minecraft, and as it comes to Windows 10 computers everywhere (and hopefully next-gen consoles like the Xbox Series X), players are in for a serious treat.</p> \n   <h4>Are you excited for ray tracing in Minecraft? Are you prepared for its arrival? Let us know in the comments below!</h4> \n   <div class=\"media-gallery-wrap\">\n    <div class=\"media-gallery\"> \n     <a size of insects.</li>\n<li>It's already attracted tons of players, and has received a few updates, including new features, since its launch.</li>\n<li>A new patch update is available today, update 0.2.1, for this early access title, and includes a sizeable list of fixes.</li>\n<li>You can find the changelog below to see if any issues you've been facing were fixed in this update.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>It feels like it hasn't been long since <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/grounded\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Grounded</a>'s first <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/grounded-august-content-update\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">content update in August</a>, and the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/grounded-early-access\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Early Access and Game Preview</a> game from Obsidian Entertainment is already getting its next patch update with version <a href=\"https://grounded.obsidian.net/news/grounded/patch-0-2-1-has-been-released\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">0.2.1</a>. This update doesn't include any new features, of course, but there are tons of bug fixes and general improvements aiming to make Grounded a better and more stable game. A lot of these fixes were requested by the community, and were <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/grounded-known-issues-and-bugs\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">known bugs and issues</a> in Grounded.</p>\n\n<p>If you're interested, the 0.2.1 patch update for Grounded includes:</p>\n\n<h3>Top community issues</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>The chat log will now show your own messages in the lobby and in the game</li>\n<li>Ants will no longer be able to steal items from containers out of reach from them</li>\n<li>You can now overwrite saved games</li>\n<li>Save Games are grouped by playthrough in the Save / Load menu</li>\n<li>Fixed an issue where the camera would go inside the player while in the 3rd-person camera when near specific building structures</li>\n<li>Grub audio has been adjusted</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3>Performance</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Better render performance when dealing with dynamic shadow culling</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3>Major</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Added a message that will notify PC players when their system clock does not match the server clock. This issue prevented these players from hosting or joining games</li>\n<li>Save Games now show an icon indicating if that save was made while playing single-player or multiplayer. Affects only new saves going forward</li>\n<li>More accurate handling of cloud save upload / deletion for Xbox and Win 10 Store versions of the game</li>\n<li>Save Game max storage on Xbox / Windows 10 has been increased from 256 MB to 1GB (takes effect on reinstall)</li>\n<li>Fixed issue with saves triggered while having an unplaced building blueprint could cause the save not to be able to load</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3>General</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Included gas damage effect that was missing from the Fresh Defense mutation</li>\n<li>Fixed items that are moving around with physics at the time of save not being saved into save games</li>\n<li>Fixed clients not being able to see other players aim their bodies when they look up and down</li>\n<li>Added Acorn Shovel+ recipe and Pebblet Foundation recipes that will become available at BURG.L's Tech Chip Swap Shop when completing the Chipslueth Cold Blooded BURG.L quest by turning in the Stained BURG.L Chip</li>\n<li>Enlarged mint container and resized the mints to make them slightly smaller so players can get into the Ice Cap container more easily</li>\n<li>Collectible SCA.Bs properly disappear on clients when picked up</li>\n<li>Included a fix for the missing leaves throughout the world</li>\n<li>Slime Mold Stalk patches properly disappear on clients when the entire stalk is collected</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3>Wildlife</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Water Fleas no longer leave the water to fly around the backyard</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3>Items / equipment / resources</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Added a unique icon to the Simple Bed</li>\n<li>Gas Arrows can now be picked up as regular arrows after being shot</li>\n<li>Gas Arrows now deal twice as much damage</li>\n<li>Gas Arrow recipe now produces 2 arrows instead of 1</li>\n<li>Feather Arrow recipe now produces 2 arrows instead of 1</li>\n<li>Fixed an issue where players would respawn inside the Simple Bed instead of next to it</li>\n<li>Weapons now do the proper damage type when thrown</li>\n<li>Fixed Tropicop juice box not spawning juice drops from the straw</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3>UI</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Adjusted the interactable highlight to be less intrusive</li>\n<li>Fixed a certain key item showing an audio log model instead of a sheet of paper model</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Overall, this is a pretty decent patch update for Grounded, even if it's not <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/grounded-next-content-update\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">the next content update</a>. While they may have some premium products for diehard fans, the TMX is a perfectly acceptable entry-level wheel that manages to retain many of the great features and design integrity of other Thrustmaster wheels.</p>\n\n<p>The TMX comes complete with a 900-degree rotation, leather trim, and paddle shifts, which are big pluses for those looking to up their racing game. serious investment for some, but there may be some players who simply want to pick one up and have some fun while racing every now and again. For those, Hori's Overdrive wheel may be the best option, as it provides an incredibly affordable price, albeit with some limitations.</p>\n\n<p>Unlike most of the other racing wheels listed here, the Hori Racing Wheel Overdrive only supports 270-degree rotation, which isn't a whole lot but should be enough for mostly every racing game, including Project Cars 3. It comes equipped with adjustable output options and a mount security for those who may need to secure their wheel somewhere.</p>\n\n<p>However, the biggest drawback to the Overdrive is the fact that it's not compatible with PC. This means that if you're looking to pick up this wheel for Project Cars 3 or any other racing game, you'll have to be sure that you're playing on an Xbox One.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Fantastic price</li>\n<li>Licensed by Microsoft</li>\n<li>Grippy rubber trim</li>\n<li>Solid build quality</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Only two-pedal setup</li>\n<li>Rotation limited to 270-degrees</li>\n<li>Not compatible with PC </li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Budget</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Hori Racing Wheel Overdrive</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-race-wheel-project-cars-3-xbox-and-pc\" title=\"Best Race Wheel for Project Cars 3 on Xbox and PC 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2019/04/hori-rwo-wheel-se-crop.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">A super-affordable way to get into using a wheel</p>\n\n<p>An incredibly affordable way to have a more immersive and enjoyable experience in your Xbox One racing games.</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Racing-Wheel-Overdrive-Officially-Licensed-Microsoft/dp/B01N5QBT08/?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU80123YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$100 at Amazon</a></p>\n\n<h2>Best Direct Drive: <em>Fanatec Podium Racing Wheel Formula</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-race-wheel-project-cars-3-xbox-and-pc\" title=\"Best Race Wheel for Project Cars 3 on Xbox and PC 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/05/dd1_reflection.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>The final wheel on our list is one that's meant for those who take racing games and simulations extremely serious. A direct drive wheel attaches the wheel right onto the motor, resulting in the highest quality force feedback, unlimited rotation, and the best accuracy that you'll get on any wheel.</p>\n\n<p>As far as features go, the Podium is packed with them. It boasts peak torque of 20nm and a holding torque of 15nm, a built-in hub, carbon fiber, and Alcantara in its construction and a built-in OLED display on the base for easy tuning. There's also a wide variety of mappable buttons, as well as an integrated display on the wheel itself.</p>\n\n<p>Of course, wheels like the Fanatec Podium Racing come at a premium, and the price tag for Fanatec's wheel is incredibly high as far as all things are considered. However, the Podium does support both Xbox and PlayStation 4 along with PC, making it an extremely versatile option for those who are seriously ready to dive into the world of racing simulators.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Ultimate realism</li>\n<li>Superb build quality</li>\n<li>Also supports console</li>\n<li>Ecosystem of accessories </li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Incredibly expensive</li>\n<li>Pedals aren't included</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Direct Drive</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Fanatec Podium Racing Wheel F1</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-race-wheel-project-cars-3-xbox-and-pc\" title=\"Best Race Wheel for Project Cars 3 on Xbox and PC 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/05/fanatecx-podium-wheel-reco-xbox.png\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://fanatec.com/us-en/racing-wheels-wheel-bases/racing-wheels/podium-racing-wheel-formula-for-xbox-one-pc\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$1,650 at Fanatec</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Like driving the real thing in the comfort of your home</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Direct drive wheels require a significant investment, but the realism is worth it with Fanatec's system.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Racing best on Xbox One</h2>\n\n<p>With the next-generation of consoles on the horizon and games like Project Cars 3 out already, racing simulators have likely never been in a better place then they are now. While it's perfectly possible to jump into the game and have fun with a controller, those looking for racing wheels also have some of the best variety of all time as it stands, but the incredible <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Logitech-Dual-Motor-Feedback-Driving-Responsive/dp/B00Z0UWV98/?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU80123YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Logitech G920</a> stands above the rest.</p>\n\n<p>Not only is it well designed and beautifully made, but it's priced very competitively as well, and comes with a full three-pedal setup that will ensure that you won't have to upgrade anytime soon. It might not sport the most complete set of features and realism, but it does come equipped with enough to make it one of the most attractive options in a sea of racing wheels.</p>\n\n<p>Both beginners and seasoned veterans of racing games will be excited about this wheel, and thanks to Logitech's excellent track record, the G920 should make for a significant investment as we head into a future of even better racing titles.</p>\n\n<h2 class=\"no-amazon\">Credits — The team that worked on this guide</h2>\n\n<p class=\"credit\"><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-race-wheel-project-cars-3-xbox-and-pc\" title=\"Best Race Wheel for Project Cars 3 on Xbox and PC 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/07/anthony-nash.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"end\"><strong>Anthony Nash</strong> is a freelance writer covering all things gaming on Android Central. Sure, it's old technology at this point, but with high-capacity SSDs still costing significantly more in some cases, it's no wonder that HDDs have stuck around. <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/dp/B07H28QRKS?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Seagate's FireCuda</a> is still one of the best ones you can buy right now. Its flash-accelerated disk means that load times ought to be faster than traditional hard drives, and it goes up to a 2TB capacity. It also comes in either a 3.5-inch or a compact 2.5-inch size, meaning it'll fit nicely in your case or enclosure.</p>\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Best Overall: <em>Seagate FireCuda</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/field/image/2018/07/seagate-firecuda-2.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Not quite a hard drive, not quite an SSD, the Seagate FireCuda blends both storage types into one unit, an SSHD, if you will. It features an embedded 8GB NAND along with up to 2TB of traditional storage to create an enhanced drive. The flash unit speeds up read/write speeds. With SATA 6Gb/s support onboard, Seagate promises a 140MB/s read speed. At 5400rpm, the drive itself is quieter and generates less heat.</p>\n\n<p>The benefits of the 8GB NAND aren't always readily apparent since the drive effectively learns your most used applications and loads them faster. For games, it might help with initial load times after you've launched the game a few times. It's easy to get excited about the possibilities with this drive, but even a SATA SSD will still outpace it by a considerable margin.</p>\n\n<p>The whole point of the FireCuda is to enhance the traditional mechanical hard drive. You can still get higher capacities without breaking the bank, all while experiencing improved performance that is noticeably better than even a 7200rpm HDD.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Great value</li>\n<li>Faster than traditional HDDs</li>\n<li>Five-year warranty</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Still outclassed by SSDs</li>\n<li>Flash-acceleration results don't always appear immediately</li>\n<li>Not as many storage options</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Overall</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">Seagate FireCuda</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/07/seagate-firecuda-2tb-sshd-cropped-33ti.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<ul class=\"cta shop\" rel=\"nofollow\">\n<li><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/dp/B07H28QRKS/ref=twister_B082N84NZ2?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">From $50 at Amazon</a></li>\n</ul>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Faster than an HDD</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">The FireCuda is the perfect option if you want an inexpensive storage option that blends HDD and SSD technology into one package.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Runner-up: <em>Western Digital Black</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/wd_black-3.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Western Digital's cream of the crop, the Black line, represents some of the best the company has to offer with traditional mechanical hard drives. While not the fastest performer, outdone by both the FireCuda and WD VelociRaptor, the Black drives are trustworthy and reliable. They're great for game storage, especially titles that don't need to load super quick like single-player games.</p>\n\n<p>In a world where the FireCuda SSHD doesn't exist, the WD Black would be my top choice, not only for its performance and reliability but also for its price. More expensive than its Blue cousin — which we'll get to in a bit — the Black still represents a tremendous performance-to-value ratio.</p>\n\n<p>Thankfully, Western Digital dropped the \"Caviar\" moniker, opting for just naming its HDD lines by their respective colors. You can start at as little as 500GB or get up to 6TB, depending on your budget. These are the drives I run in my rig, and I've never had a problem. If you're worried, WD throws in a five-year warranty.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Great value</li>\n<li>Reliable</li>\n<li>Five-year warranty</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Can get loud</li>\n<li>Outpaced by the FireCuda</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Runner-up</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">WD Black</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/wd_black.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Black-Performance-Desktop-Hard-Drive/dp/B00FJRS628?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $55 at Amazon</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">A solid performer</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Western Digital's flagship HDD line, the Black, is an excellent drive for storing games and other media.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Best Storage: <em>Seagate BarraCuda Pro</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/barracuda_pro-3.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>In a similar vein to the WD Black, we have the Seagate BarraCuda Pro series of mechanical hard drives. Sporting Seagate's most robust reliability claims and a higher warranty than the regular BarraCuda — again, we'll get to that shortly — the Pro series aims to last for years to come.</p>\n\n<p>The BarraCuda Pro features a 300TB/year workload maximum, so like the WD Black, it's best left for things like games where you're not going to be moving them back and forth. It's a 7200rpm drive that supports SATA 6Gb/s for that fast transfer speed.</p>\n\n<p>Where the BarraCuda Pro outclasses, the WD Black is the storage options available. You start at 2TB and can climb up to a ludicrous 14TB. You'll pay a pretty penny for that much space, though.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Excellent performance</li>\n<li>Plenty of storage options</li>\n<li>Five-year warranty</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Not as good of a value as the WD Black or FireCuda</li>\n<li>Beaten by the FireCuda for speed</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Storage</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">Seagate BarraCuda Pro</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/barracuda_pro.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"http://www.amazon.com/dp/B07H24QRS1?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $120 at Amazon</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Another great HDD</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Seagate's BarraCuda Pro features more storage options that the WD Black, but comes in at a higher price.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Best Performance: <em>Western Digital VelociRaptor</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/wd_velociraptor-2.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>If you're looking for best-in-class HDD performance, then look no further than the WD VelociRaptor. Western Digital is a massive name in the hard drive market, best known for a variety of product categories, including internal hard drives. There are several different WD options — Blue for budget, Red for NAS, Black for performance, Purple for surveillance — but the 10,000rpm VelociRaptor is the king among hard disk drives.</p>\n\n<p>However, this drive is pricy and comes in lower storage sizes, not to mention the SSDs still outclass it. The 2TB Kingston A400 SSD, for example, is roughly the same price and runs laps around this drive at double the space. There's no longer a place for a drive like this.</p>\n\n<p>But, I suppose if you're set on sticking with HDDs, and don't want to go with an SSHD, then the VelociRaptor is the best you'll get in terms of performance. Western Digital also includes a five-year warranty in case anything goes wrong.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Fast 10,000rpm</li>\n<li>Five-year warranty</li>\n<li>Highly reliable</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Still outclassed by SSDs</li>\n<li>Questionable value</li>\n<li>Limited storage options</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Performance</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">WD VelociRaptor</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/wd_velociraptor.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<ul class=\"cta shop\" rel=\"nofollow\">\n<li><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Black-Performance-Desktop-Hard-Drive/dp/B00FJRS628/?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">From $45 at Amazon</a></li>\n</ul>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">High-performance at a price</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">The fastest HDD available, the WD VelociRaptor, is neat, but it's a questionable value when you consider similarly priced SSDs.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Best Value: <em>Seagate BarraCuda</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/barracuda-2.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>If you want to save money and get the best bang for your buck, then the Seagate BarraCuda is it. The value here is nothing to sneeze at. Undercutting its own Pro cousin, the regular BarraCuda packs in the same 7200rpm rotational speed, SATA 6Gb/s, and generous storage options.</p>\n\n<p>There isn't too much else to say here. Frankly, you can't beat the value of the BarraCuda, and word has it that the reliability of this drive has improved drastically in recent years. One of its most significant downsides from all reports is that it lacks robustness when it comes to random read/write speeds — arguably a better indication of real-world use.</p>\n\n<p>The BarraCuda HDD starts at 1TB and goes up to 8TB, with the value proposition getting better and better at the higher capacities.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Incredible value</li>\n<li>Plenty of storage options</li>\n<li>Two-year warranty</li>\n<li>Generally a quiet drive</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Sketchy reliability in the past</li>\n<li>Lower random read/write speeds</li>\n<li>Shorter warranty than the Pro</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Value</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">Seagate BarraCuda</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/seagate_barracuda.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<ul class=\"cta shop\" rel=\"nofollow\">\n<li><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/dp/B07D99KFPK/?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">From $45 at Amazon</a></li>\n</ul>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Best bang for your buck</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">If you need to add storage to your PC and want to keep the price down, the Seagate BarraCuda is the best option.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Most Reliable: <em>Western Digital Blue</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/wd_blue-2.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Coming in hot behind the BarraCuda is the WD Blue, Western Digital's budget line of HDDs. They're essentially comparable to the BarraCuda but generally run for a few bucks more on average. Western Digital has typically had a better reputation for reliability.</p>\n\n<p>The WD Blue is to the Black like the BarraCuda is to the Pro. Essentially, it's the same drive with a shorter warranty and a few performance tweaks left off to keep costs down. That's fine, but Western Digital needs to keep an eye out on Seagate and drop its prices a tad to stay competitive beyond simple brand loyalty.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Great value</li>\n<li>Several storage options</li>\n<li>Two-year warranty</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Slightly more expensive than Seagate</li>\n<li>Some trouble reported with the warranty</li>\n<li>Shorter warranty than the Black</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Most Reliable</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">WD Blue</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/01/wd_blue.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<ul class=\"cta shop\" rel=\"nofollow\">\n<li><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/WD-Blue-2TB-Hard-Drive/dp/B07JC1TQ7N?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">$55 at Amazon</a></li>\n</ul>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Runner-up</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">The WD Blue line is second only to the BarraCuda in terms of value.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2>Best for a NAS: <em>Seagate IronWolf</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/05/seagate_ironwolf.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>What if you're not looking for game storage, but rather something for all of your important files? That's where a NAS (network-attached storage) comes in. Whether you're building your own or buying one ready to go, you'll need some hard drives to keep everything backed up. And my pick for that is Seagate's IronWolf.</p>\n\n<p>I run these personally in my own NAS, and they're great. NAS drives are a bit different than desktop-class HDDs because they're designed to run 24/7 while maintaining a higher level of performance. According to Seagate, the IronWolf comes in storage sizes ranging from 1TB up to 16TB with a three-year warranty. There's also the IronWolf Pro line, but that's aimed more at the business and otherwise professional level.</p>\n\n<p>If you opt for the 3TB or above, you'll get Seagate's IronWolf Health Management, which works well with some NAS manufacturers to make sure that the drive is running at its best. Also, bear in mind that the 4TB drives and below run at 5,900rpm rather than 7,200rpm. The 1TB and 2TB models lack the vibration sensing features. The Pro line doesn't feature these disparities, but you pay a bit more of a premium to compensate.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Excellent value</li>\n<li>Multiple storage options</li>\n<li>Three-year warranty</li>\n<li>Solid reliability</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Lower capacity drives lack some features</li>\n<li>Shorter warranty than the IronWolf Pro</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Best for a NAS</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Seagate IronWolf</h4>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/article_images/2019/07/ironwolf-12-4lsr.jpg\" width=\"800\" height=\"1155\" alt=\"Seagate IronWolf\" title=\"\" data-source=\"Amazon\" class=\"image-large image-neutral \"></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Seagate-IronWolf-5900RPM-Internal-3-5-Inch/dp/B07H28PKLX/?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $60 at Amazon</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Great NAS performance</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">If you're building a NAS or expanding your existing one's storage, the Seagate IronWolf is the best drive for the job.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2>Best Enterprise HDD: <em>Seagate Exos X</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/05/seagate_exos_x16.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Once again, Seagate has come out with a drive that matches Western Digital's offering and beats it on price. Above the IronWolf, and even the IronWolf Pro, is the Exos X. These enterprise-grade HDDs are meant for servers and are a bit outside the scope of the consumer market unless you're a \"prosumer\" who's running a home lab or just want some of the best and most reliable performance you can get.</p>\n\n<p>The Exos X ranges from 8TB to 16TB, with the top of the line X16 models sporting 14TB and 16TB capacities. It's much easier to find the X16, though the X10 model (a few steps down) and X14 are available, too. All told, the Exos X16 can handle 550TB of workload per year and has a Mean Time Before Failure (MTBF) of <em>2.5 million hours</em>. That's pretty awesome. Seagate also includes a 5-year warranty.</p>\n\n<p>Whether you go with a Seagate or a Western Digital — or even HGST — enterprise drive depends on your brand loyalty and what's on sale when you're shopping; the performance is nearly identical between the brands. Keep in mind that these enterprise-grade drives come at quite a cost over NAS or desktop HDDs.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Good performance</li>\n<li>Five-year warranty</li>\n<li>Power efficient</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Pricey</li>\n<li>Lacks some of the IronWolf features</li>\n<li>Fewer smaller storage options</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Enterprise HDD</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Seagate Exos X</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-internal-hard-drives\" title=\"Best Internal Hard Drives (HDD) in 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/05/exos_x-2.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Seagate-12TB-7200RPM-256MB-SATA/dp/B07MRLCWSQ/?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $284 at Amazon</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Enterprise-grade</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Seagate seemingly one-upped Western Digital again with the Exos X enterprise hard drives. These go all the way up to 16TB capacities, but they're a premium.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Bottom line</h2>\n\n<p>Long gone is the heyday of HDDs, but they're still a great option if you want the best GB-to-dollar ratio. Seagate and Western Digital remain the big players in this space. Yet, ultimately, our recommendation for the best HDD for your money isn't an HDD at all, but the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/dp/B07H28QRKS?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">SSHD FireCuda</a>. It packs a great value with <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/seagate-firecuda-sshd-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">some extra performance</a>, outpacing the next runner-up.</p>\n\n<p>As I've said multiple times, a SATA SSD will still outclass each of the drives mentioned on this list, even the FireCuda, and VelociRaptor. While you don't get quite the spacious storage options, you can pick up an SSD as a boot drive for pretty cheap these days. Assuming you want to just bulk up your storage for your games library without breaking the bank, then the Seagate FireCuda is the way to go.</p>\n\n<p>And if you want to move beyond desktop-class drives for a NAS or home server rack, Seagate's got the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Seagate-IronWolf-5900RPM-Internal-3-5-Inch/dp/B07H28PKLX?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">IronWolf</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Seagate-12TB-7200RPM-256MB-SATA/dp/B07MRLCWSQ/?tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU73814YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Exos X</a> drives to do what you need them to. I run four IronWolf drives in my NAS, and I have found that they're great performers, plus they sport some useful features.</p></div></div></div><img
