field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/madden-21-details-improvements-franchise-mode-coming-next-update\" title=\"Madden 21 details improvements to Franchise mode coming in next update\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/madden-nfl-21-2.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"intro\">Fixes are on the way.</p>\n\n<h2 class=\"aside news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>Electronic Arts has detailed some of the changes coming to Madden NFL 21's Franchise Mode.</li>\n<li>Changes include a revamped stats UI, playoff brackets, and more.</li>\n<li>EA hopes to have the update out by mid-November.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>After promising to fix some of the issues regarding its longstanding Franchise Mode, Electronic Arts has recently detailed some of the changes that will be coming to <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/madden-nfl-21\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Madden NFL 21</a>'s Franchise mode in a future update.</p>\n\n<p>In a brand new <a href=\"https://www.ea.com/games/madden-nfl/madden-nfl-21/news/gridiron-notes-franchise-updates-coming-to-madden-nfl-21\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">blog post</a> detailing some of the changes, EA has announced that after some time carefully planning and implementing the changes, they have come up with some changes to the mode. This includes a re-tooled way of handling the game's X-Factor and Superstar abilities, allowing commissioners to assign X-Factors to any player, a revamped stats UI, and much more.</p>\n\n<p>Electronic Arts says that it's currently targeting a mid-November release for the patch, which will be the first of three post-launch franchise updates. According to them, users also won't have to restart a franchise to have access to the additions made in the updates, meaning that you can freely play through franchise mode now and not worry about losing any progress. In our <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/madden-nfl-21-review-familiar-face\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">review of Madden NFL 21</a>, some of the biggest issues holding the game back was its many bugs and glitches and lack of franchise mode additions, so it's nice to see EA attempting to fix things at a fairly rapid pace.</p>\n\n<p>For a more detailed look at what's coming in the new update to Franchise Mode when it drops later this year, check out below:</p>\n\n<ul>\n<li><p>X-Factor/Superstar Ability Customization: This highly requested feature by the community allows commissioners to assign X-Factors to any player via the edit player feature. Once a player has met the criteria to unlock an X-Factor ability, commissioners will be able to edit their player's Superstar abilities and Superstar X-Factor ability by selecting from those available within his position group. Users will have control over this functionality in both offline and online Franchises.</p></li>\n<li><p>Player Card Career Stats UI: A top community request for several years now, the team is revamping the statistics on the player card to include more context in season stats, like week, opponent, and outcome, while also providing what team the player was on for every year of their career.</p></li>\n<li><p>Dev Trait Regression Tuning: The team is doing tuning work to player development traits in Franchise mode to ensure a proper balance of Superstar and X-Factor players when progressing multiple years in a Franchise.</p></li>\n<li><p>Playoff Bracket: A visual playoff bracket will be added into the game that reflects the new Wild Card format, allowing users to see the full playoff picture.</p></li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Madden NFL 21 is currently available on Xbox One, PlayStation 4, and PC.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Go Nash","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/madden-nfl-21-2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn100@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-44-12-492_03cb5c4a2e9286bd.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/madden-nfl-21-box-art.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn98@2020_4/2020/09/05/08-44-17-210_b9de6efa773ebf4a.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/wmexperts/~4/sClcGf7BM9w":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn58@2020_5/2020/09/05/08-44-14-475_14e1f724a4a6bc3e.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1599295452307},{"createdTime":"2020-09-05 16:44:12","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:44:12","title":"Tips for handling Microsoft Flight Simulator's landing challenges","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/JFY5tjQ_hsk/microsoft-flight-simulator-landing-challenge-tips-and-tricks","description":"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-landing-challenge-tips-and-tricks\" title=\"Microsoft Flight Simulator: Landing challenge tips and tricks\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/microsoft-flight-simulator-airbus-a320-jfk.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Microsoft Flight Simulator is the latest entry in Microsoft's long-running Flight Simulator series and is easily the most impressive. Using cloud-based technology, data streams in real-time.  The game uses AI to extrapolate geometry, landscaping, foliage density, meteorological data, and air traffic updates. These features make every flight feel as real as possible. Yes, you can really see your house from up there, and you can also see what the weather's like as well.</p>\n\n<p>Microsoft Flight Simulator offers 24 landing challenges that task players with landing specific aircraft in a variety of locations, from the most popular airports to the most dangerous landing strips in the world. The goal is to land the plane as smoothly and as accurately as possible. You're graded on how close to the center of the runway you land, how long it takes your plane to come to a full stop, and the touchdown's smoothness. Also, there are no assists in this mode — you'll have to manage it all by yourself. Trying to land your plane is difficult, so here are some tips and tricks that will make the landing challenges a little less scary.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">The Latest and Greatest</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Microsoft Flight Simulator</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-landing-challenge-tips-and-tricks\" title=\"Microsoft Flight Simulator: Landing challenge tips and tricks\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/microsoft-flight-simulator-2020-box-art-square.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU80069YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fp%252Fmicrosoft-flight-simulator-standard---preorder%252F9NXN8GF8N9HT&#38;token=z31zfS3z\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $60 at Microsoft</a>\n<a href=\"https://store.steampowered.com/app/1250410/Microsoft_Flight_Simulator/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">From $60 at Steam</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Microsoft Flight Simulator 2020 offers a cloud-powered globe, with authenticity on an unmatched scale. It's available exclusively for Windows PCs.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2>Go through with the tutorial</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-landing-challenge-tips-and-tricks\" title=\"Microsoft Flight Simulator: Landing challenge tips and tricks\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/microsoft-flight-simulator-2.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>This is a no brainer, but it's probably the most critical step in this game. Getting into the sky is much easier said than done. Microsoft Flight Simulator is not a game where you can jump into the cockpit and wing it. It offers an extensive training program that'll teach you the ins and outs of a Cessna 152. You'll learn the fundamentals of plane control, flight instruments, and other essential basics before concluding training with a full takeoff and landing.</p>\n\n<p>The most useful tutorial level for prepping for landing challenges is the fourth tutorial; it's all about landing. If you are having trouble, replay that level until you've got it down to a science. Each plane handles differently, but being comfortable in the cockpit is the first step to learning and mastering the other airplanes and beating their respective challenges.</p>\n\n<h2>Master your control</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-landing-challenge-tips-and-tricks\" title=\"Microsoft Flight Simulator: Landing challenge tips and tricks\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/microsoft-flight-simulator-tbm-snow.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Microsoft Flight Simulator is playable with an Xbox controller, a mouse and keyboard, or if you're really serious about flying, a combination of a <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-yokes-microsoft-flight-simulator\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">yoke</a> and a pair of pedals. Learning the subtleties of an aircraft takes time, and if you're having trouble wrapping your head around everything, I found that breaking out an Xbox controller helped me out a lot. If you do go that route, turn the sensitivity down.</p>\n\n<p>The default sensitivity is fine, but for the challenges that involve heavy winds, you'll find yourself swinging back and forth while flying. When you want to make smaller adjustments to your aircraft, you're going to want more sensitive controls. Here's how to find them.</p>\n\n<ol>\n<li>Find the Controls in the <strong>Options tab</strong> in the main menu.</li>\n<li>Click on your controller input, and find Sensitivity on the <strong>left side of the screen</strong>.</li>\n</ol>\n\n<p>Dropping the sensitivity down by at least 10% helps a lot, but you can afford to drop it further for smaller aircraft, which are a lot more sensitive. It helps to set up profiles based on the plane you're flying, so you can easily swap sensitivity when you swap planes.</p>\n\n<h2>Stay on target</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-landing-challenge-tips-and-tricks\" title=\"Microsoft Flight Simulator: Landing challenge tips and tricks\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/microsoft-flight-simulator-1.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Landing in Microsoft Flight Simulator might be the hardest thing you do on your whole flight; there are so many things that can go wrong. You could come in too fast, or too slow, or at the wrong angle. While there are no crash animations in the game, the black screen that hits after a crash somehow hurts even more.</p>\n\n<p>The key to landing is to maintain about 65 knots; target the number at the front of the runway in your dashboard. Begin descending on a path where that number stays as level as it can. If the number is rising, then you're falling too quickly, and you need more throttle. If it's falling, you're flying too fast, and you'll want to reduce your speed. Target the middle of the runway and point the nose of the aircraft down. Just as you're about to make contact with the runway, pull the nose of the aircraft up gently, and the plane should hit the ground with no problem.</p>\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">Practice makes perfect</h2>\n\n<p>The landing challenges are a fun way to try out all of the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/list-microsoft-flight-simulator-planes\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">different planes</a> available and learn how they handle. With some practice, you'll be able to make smooth and safe landings all over the world — maybe even take a trip into the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-let-people-fly-hurricane-laura\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">eye of a storm</a>! What works best for you when tackling the landing challenges? Do you have any other tips worth sharing? Let us know in the comments.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">The Latest and Greatest</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Microsoft Flight Simulator</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-landing-challenge-tips-and-tricks\" title=\"Microsoft Flight Simulator: Landing challenge tips and tricks\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/microsoft-flight-simulator-2020-box-art-square.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU80069YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fp%252Fmicrosoft-flight-simulator-standard---preorder%252F9NXN8GF8N9HT&#38;token=z31zfS3z\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $60 at Microsoft</a>\n<a href=\"https://store.steampowered.com/app/1250410/Microsoft_Flight_Simulator/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">From $60 at Steam</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Microsoft Flight Simulator 2020 offers a cloud-powered globe, with authenticity on an unmatched scale. significant bugs and performance issues have kept players from really loving their adventures in post-apocalyptic Colorado. Luckily some big fixes are on the way via inXile Entertainment's first major patch for the game.</p>\n\n<p>Patch 1.1.0 is expected to be available to PC players via Steam and GOG today and will be coming to Xbox One and PS4 by the middle of next week. The release follows a previous hotfix that significantly improved the game's performance on consoles.</p>\n\n<p>The developers prioritized the biggest blocking issues that players have reported, though they promise that fixes for plenty of other problems will be released in the next few weeks. While the patch notes will provide a more in-depth description of the bugs being squashed, here's a list of some of the biggest issues that are being fixed:</p>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Intro movie not playing for the host in co-op or one player being stuck watching the cinematic</li>\n<li>Load screens stalling at 33%</li>\n<li>Progression blocked for players with systems set to some regions or languages</li>\n<li>Syncing radio transmissions in co-op and preventing the Kodiak from de-syncing after they're received</li>\n<li>Blocked La Perla quest</li>\n<li>Fishlips encounter</li>\n<li>Improved toughness for Polly and Cyborg Chickens</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>While you're waiting for the patch, you can check out <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/known-bugs-and-issues-wasteland-3\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">our list</a> of known issues and bugs, which also provides some workarounds. href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/pentagon-sticking-microsoft-10-billion-jedi-cloud-contract-after-review\" title=\"Pentagon sticking with Microsoft for $10 billion JEDI cloud contract after review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/field/image/2018/03/microsoft-logo-ignite-2017.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"intro\">There's still a long legal battle ahead.</p>\n\n<h2 class=\"aside news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>The Pentagon today reaffirmed its decision to award Microsoft a $10 billion cloud contract.</li>\n<li>The JEDI contract in question has come under intense scrutiny ever since Microsoft beat Amazon out for the bid.</li>\n<li>The contract is still on hold after a court challenge by Amazon earlier this year.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>The Pentagon today announced that it still plans to continue work on the Joint Enterprise Defense Infrastructure (JEDI) contract with Microsoft after completing a re-evaluation of proposals. The deal will see Microsoft working with the Department of Defense (DoD) to modernize its IT infrastructure. The contract was awarded to Microsoft in 2019, a decision that was challenged by Amazon, who was among the bidders.</p>\n\n<p>In a statement issued today, <a href=\"https://www.defense.gov/Newsroom/Releases/Release/Article/2337557/dod-reaffirms-original-jedi-cloud-award-to-microsoft/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">DoD said</a>:</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>The Department has completed its comprehensive re-evaluation of the JEDI Cloud proposals and determined that Microsoft's proposal continues to represent the best value to the Government.  The JEDI Cloud contract is a firm-fixed-price, indefinite-delivery/indefinite-quantity contract that will make a full range of cloud computing services available to the DoD.  While contract performance will not begin immediately due to the Preliminary Injunction Order issued by the Court of Federal Claims on February 13, 2020, DoD is eager to begin delivering this capability to our men and women in uniform.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>\"We appreciate that after careful review, the DoD confirmed that we offered the right technology and the best value,\" a Microsoft spokesperson told <a href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2020/09/04/pentagon-says-it-will-stick-with-microsoft-for-jedi-cloud-contract.html\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">CNBC</a>. \"We're ready to get to work and make sure that those who serve our country have access to this much needed technology.\"</p>\n\n<p>As the DoD notes, the contract is still on hold due to an injunction issued earlier this year. The court proceeding was initiated by Amazon, another bidder in the selection process, which claims that the DoD's decision was influenced by bias against Amazon and its CEO, Jeff Bezos, by President Donald Trump.</p>\n\n<p>In a <a href=\"https://aws.amazon.com/blogs/publicsector/jedi-why-we-will-continue-protest-politically-corrupted-contract-award/\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">lengthy blog post</a> responding to DoD's decision, Amazon stated:</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>When the DoD announced its plans for corrective action in March, we objected because it was clear this was nothing more than a \"do-over\" for Microsoft to fix its non-compliant proposal. Given the DoD did not agree to meaningfully review the many evaluation flaws outlined in our protest, we said the corrective action was likely to result in another contract award based on politics and improper influence and not based on the relative strengths of the two offerings. That is exactly where we find ourselves today, with the DoD's re-evaluation nothing more than an attempt to validate a flawed, biased, and politically corrupted decision. It's also important to point out that the DoD cited price as a major factor in the previous decision. This time, AWS offered a lower cost by several tens of millions of dollars. The DoD's decision to intentionally ignore the clear cost benefits offered by AWS, reinforces the fact that this corrective action was never meant to be fair.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>While the JEDI contract is held up in courts, recent reporting suggests Microsoft is currently pursuing <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-seeks-expand-jedi-cloud-contracts-foreign-governments\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">similar contracts</a> with foreign governments.</p></div></div></div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/wmexperts/~4/4wqvUJRa6g8\" height=\"1\" while to go before they can order a Surface Duo.</p>\n\n<h2 class=\"aside news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>The Surface Duo might not ship outside of the United States until 2021.</li>\n<li>The plan for the Surface Duo is fluid and could change as circumstances change.</li>\n<li>The Surface Duo already has certifications in Canada, the EU, and Japan.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Last month, Microsoft disappointed thousands of fans who have been eagerly waiting for the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Surface Duo</a> by announcing that the product would be launching exclusively in the United States, with no plans to bring it to other markets for the foreseeable future. Adding insult to injury, Microsoft refused to provide any kind of timeframe for the fans who have been saving to buy one.</p>\n\n<p>In the United States, customers can <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU80156YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fsurface%252Fdevices%252Fsurface-duo&#38;token=5ygluTE-\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">pre-order the Surface Duo</a> now for $1,399 and have it by September 10. Outside the United States, customers have simply been told that Microsoft is taking \"a measured and phased approach to availability to meet customer demand.\" Essentially, Microsoft doesn't want to make too many and sell too few.</p>\n\n<p>Of course, this is a valid concern for Microsoft to have. It doesn't want another Surface RT failure by building more devices than it can sell. But, as one of the Surface Duo's biggest followers that also resides outside the United States, I've been extremely disappointed with Microsoft's lack of real communication regarding its plans for Surface Duo elsewhere in the world.</p>\n\n<p>I've since done some digging, and according to my sources Microsoft is looking to begin shipping Surface Duo in external markets in the first half of 2021 after seeing if the product surpasses internal expectations in the United States first. This plan is fluid, however, and Microsoft could decide to bring its release in other markets forward if circumstances change.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-specs-camera-ram-storage-soc-battery#:~:text=Surface%20Duo%20specs%20%20%20%20Category%20,256GB%20UFS%203.0%20%2013%20more%20rows%20\" title=\"\" class=\"cta large norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Surface Duo specs</a></p>\n\n<p>The longer Microsoft waits, the harder it will be to sell a product with a Snapdragon 855 with 6GB RAM and without wireless charging or NFC capabilities to new customers. class=\"intro\">What's going on with 2K Sports' first PGA Tour title?</p> \n   <p>In 2018, 2K Sports announced that it had taken over publishing for The Golf Club series of games, formally changing its name to PGA Tour 2K. With the first title, PGA Tour 2K21, set to launch next month, more and more information about the game is beginning to come out, giving us a great idea of what golfing with 2K Sports will look like.</p> \n   <p>Here's everything we know so far about the golf game and what you can expect to see in it.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/pga-tour-2k21-review-golf-game-everybody\" title=\"\" class=\"cta large norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Related: PGA Tour 2K21 Review: A Golf game for <!--sectionbreak--> \n   <h2 id=\"pga\">What is <em>PGA Tour 2K21</em>?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/pga-2k21\" title=\"PGA 2K21: Everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/pga-tour-2k21-1.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>PGA Tour 2K21 is the latest entry in a series of golf video games that were initially known as The Golf Club. After creating three entries in that series, with the latest being The Golf Club featuring PGA Tour, 2K Sports announced that it took over publishing rights and promptly changed the games name to PGA Tour 2K21.</p> \n   <p>Much like other sports titles, PGA Tour 2K21 promises to offer a realistic simulation golf experience, allowing players to feel like they're really out on the course while playing. PGA Tour 2K21 will feature 12 PGA Tour pros, including the cover star Justin Thomas, and will also feature a PGA Tour career mode, course designer, and much more when it launches.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"gameplay\">What is PGA Tour 2K21's <em>gameplay</em> like?</h2> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/4g0ZWHYyXGA?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-4g0zwhyyxga\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>Similar to other golfing video games, PGA Tour 2K21 will focus heavily on the realistic aspects of golf, including choosing which club to use at various points in the game, timing up shots, and more. In a brief gameplay trailer released by 2K Sports, we also get to see what the overhead camera will look like, which will allow players to get a better look at what type of terrain they will be hitting the ball onto.</p> \n   <p>One of the key aspects to being a successful golfer is how you handle a putt, and PGA Tour 2K21 looks to have that covered as well. Once on the green, PGA Tour 2K21 has a grid cover the entire green, giving you a good layout of the angles and incline of the patch of grass you'll be shooting over. It isn't revolutionary by any means, but it is good to see PGA Tour 2K21 giving players the full golfing experience that fans have come to expect.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"consoles\">What <em>game modes</em> does PGA Tour 2K21 have?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/pga-2k21\" title=\"PGA 2K21: Everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/pga-tour-2k21-2.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>The <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/nba-2k21\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NBA 2K series</a> has become known for its wide variety of game modes and features, and it looks like PGA Tour 2K21 will be no different. Players will be able to hit the links with their friends in local and online multiplayer, run full seasons and tournaments with the Online Societies feature, and also be able to play out their dreams of becoming a PGA Tour Champion with the all new PGA Tour Career Mode.</p> \n   <p>Much like the MyCareer mode in the NBA 2K series, the PGA Tour Career Mode will allow players to create their own character and take them from humble beginnings to the ranks of greatest golfer ever. Throughout the mode, you'll customize your MyPlayers appearance, skill, and much more, all while trying to take down the games 12 other professional golfers as you strive to become the FedEx Cup Champion.</p> \n   <p>PGA Tour 2K21 also promises to have some other modes that fans may love, including a course design mode that lets you create your own golf course. This will give players the chance to recreate some of the most iconic courses in golf history, as well as make some fun and less traditional courses as well.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"myplayer\">Will PGA 2K21 have a <em>MyPlayer</em> feature?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/pga-2k21\" title=\"PGA 2K21: Everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/06/pga-tour-2k21-hero.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Thanks to HB Studios partnering with 2K Sports, PGA Tour 2K21 will feature some things that fans of the NBA 2K series will recognize. Along with an overhauled Career mode, PGA 2K21 will also include the ability for players to create their own MyPlayer. Similar to how 2K usually operates, players can choose from a variety of preset options, or build their own golfer from scratch. Customizing the height, weight, gender, and other features will allow players to make the perfect counterpart for themselves.</p> \n   <p>Just like the NBA 2K series, everyones MyPlayer will be available across all of PGA 2K21's game modes, including its multiplayer modes and Career mode. Alongside being able to create your own MyPlayer, PGA 2K21 also includes a ton of apparel and gear upgrades that can be made throughout your time playing. Whether it be earning awards through sponsorships or performing well in various tournaments, your MyPlayer will be a huge part of how you play PGA 2K21.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"golfers\">Are there professional golfers in PGA 2K21?</h2> \n   <p>While previous iterations of The Golf Club franchise didn't have any professional golfers for players to go up against, HB Studios fixed that. In PGA Tour 2K21, players will be able to go up against 12 real world professional golfers, including Justin Thomas, the current #1 ranked golfer in the world. Alongside being in the game, the professionals will also serve as rivals to your MyPlayer, with players being able to form rivalries with various stars and take them on throughout your Career. Outperforming your rivals can result in big rewards for you, and getting to see real pros actually participate in the game is a huge step forward for the franchise.</p> \n   <p>The full list of PGA Tour professionals that have been scanned into the game include:</p> \n   <ul> \n    <li>Justin Thomas</li> \n    <li>Cameron Champ</li> \n    <li>Bryson DeChambeau</li> \n    <li>Matt Kuchar</li> \n    <li>Kevin Kisner</li> \n    <li>Gary Woodland</li> \n    <li>Billy Horschel</li> \n    <li>Ian Poulter</li> \n    <li>Tony Finau</li> \n    <li>Jim Furyk</li> \n    <li>Sergio Garcia</li> \n    <li>Patrick Cantlay</li> \n   </ul> \n   <h2 id=\"courses\">How many courses are there in PGA 2K21?</h2> \n   <p>PGA Tour 2K21 will feature 15 officially licensed courses when the game launches. A handful of courses - including Detroit Golf Club and Rocket Mortgage Classic - are planned for post-launch, giving players a ton of places to experience and play.</p> \n   <p>The full list of available courses in the game can be found below:</p> \n   <ul> \n    <li>Atlantic Beach Country Club</li> \n    <li>Copperhead Course (Innisbrook)</li> \n    <li>East Lake Golf Club</li> \n    <li>Quail Hollow Club</li> \n    <li>Riviera Country Club</li> \n    <li>TPC Boston</li> \n    <li>TPC Deere Run</li> \n    <li>TPC Louisiana</li> \n    <li>TPC River Highlands</li> \n    <li>TPC San Antonio</li> \n    <li>TPC Sawgrass</li> \n    <li>TPC Scottsdale</li> \n    <li>TPC Southwind</li> \n    <li>TPC Summerlin</li> \n    <li>TPC Twin Cities</li> \n   </ul> \n   <h2 id=\"release\">When is the <em>release date</em>?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/pga-2k21\" title=\"PGA 2K21: Everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/pga-tour-2k21-3.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>PGA Tour 2K21 is now available for PlayStation 4, Xbox One, Nintendo Switch, Google Stadia, and PC.</p> \n   <!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Go pro</h3> \n   <h4 class=\"product\">PGA Tour 2K21</h4> \n   <p><a based on budget and required performance. You can mix and match hardware as you please and still end up with a powerful rig. For most people, the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fnvidia-geforce-rtx-2080-super-8gb-gddr6-pci-express-3-0-graphics-card-black-silver%252F6361326.p%253FskuId%253D6361326&amp;token=kCGbq6EW\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA GeForce RTX 2080 Super</a> is going to hit a high-end performance tier and not cost an excessive amount of money like the more powerful overkill option, the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D44583%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.newegg.com%252Fasus-geforce-rtx-2080-ti-rog-strix-rtx2080ti-o11g-gaming%252Fp%252FN82E16814126263&amp;token=pUk7PAZ0\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA GeForce RTX 2080 Ti</a>. If you're looking to experience 4K gaming, either GPU will work well. If you want to just dabble in 4K gaming but primarily focus on a high-end 1440p experience, the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fnvidia-geforce-rtx-2070-super-8gb-gddr6-pci-express-3-0-graphics-card-black-silver%252F6361328.p%253FskuId%253D6361328&amp;token=QiklBBg9\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA RTX 2070 Super</a> will do good for those on Team Green while the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Sapphire-11293-01-20G-Radeon-Backplate-Graphics/dp/B07WC7683C?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44996YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">AMD Radeon RX 5700 XT</a> will be attractive for those on Team Red.</p> \n    <p>There are plenty more best graphics card options out there, whether you're looking at one for gaming, 4K power, or happen to be on a budget. And don't forget to keep an eye out for the latest <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/nvidia-unveils-rtx-3090-rtx-3080-rtx-3070-pricing-details-availability\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA RTX 30-series GPUs</a>, which will undoubtedly move into the top spots when they are released. Availability for the RTX 3080 is expected to begin September 17, with the RTX 3070 and RTX 3090 expected to follow shortly after. Until then, these are the best graphics card options available.</p> \n    <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fnvidia-geforce-rtx-2080-super-8gb-gddr6-pci-express-3-0-graphics-card-black-silver%252F6361326.p%253FskuId%253D6361326&amp;token=kCGbq6EW\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" title=\"Best Graphics Card 2020: Top GPUs for Gaming\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/nvidia-geforce-rtx-2080-super-founders-best-hero-02.png\" /></a></p> \n    <h2 id=\"2080S\">1. NVIDIA GeForce RTX 2080 Super: <em>Best Graphics Card for Most Gamers</em></h2> \n    <p><strong>Bottom line:</strong> Thanks to powerful performance and a relatively reasonable price, the RTX 2080 Super is an excellent pick for most people. It affords you the ability to choose FHD, QHD, or UHD resolutions at a high frame rate, and it delivers the extra features exclusive to NVIDIA RTX cards like <strong>ray tracing</strong> and <strong>deep-learning super sampling (DLSS) 2.0</strong>. It doesn't quite deliver the same performance as the mighty RTX 2080 Ti, but it also costs hundreds less and won't be quite as overkill for most people's needs.</p> \n    <p><strong>Memory:</strong> href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fgoto.walmart.com%2Fc%2F1943169%2F612734%2F9383%3Fsharedid%3D159229%26subId1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.walmart.com%252Fip%252FEVGA-GeForce-RTX-2080-Super-XC-Ultra-Gaming-Graphics-Card%252F402523674&amp;token=uAGAmUz-\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop no-alt-cta norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$900 at Walmart</a></td> \n      </tr> \n     </tbody> \n    </table> \n    <p class=\"caption\">We recommend checking out the <strong>NVIDIA Founders Edition</strong> version due to solid all-around performance and unbeatable price.</p> \n    <h3 class=\"pros\">Pros</h3> \n    <ul> \n     <li>48 dedicated ray-tracing cores</li> \n     <li>AI-enhancements from DLSS 2.0</li> \n     <li>Compatible with G-Sync displays</li> \n     <li>Powerful enough for 4K gaming</li> \n     <li>Much better price than RTX 2080 Ti</li> \n    </ul> \n    <h3 class=\"cons\">Cons</h3> \n    <ul> \n     <li>Overkill for some people</li> \n     <li>Relatively expensive</li> \n    </ul> \n    <p>There's no one true pick for everyone when it comes to the <em>best graphics card</em>, but if we're choosing what should suit most people based on performance and price, we have to go with <strong>NVIDIA's GeForce RTX 2080 Super</strong>. While AMD has undoubtedly cut into NVIDIA's claim to the GPU throne with its Radeon RX 5000 cards, a few of which are included in this roundup, the top-tier options still belong to Team Green. The RTX 2080 Super isn't the <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/44JGrw-4ZQo/best-graphics-cards#2080TI\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">most powerful GPU in this roundup</a>, but it still delivers smooth 4K performance for hundreds of dollars less.</p> \n    <p>The RTX 2080 Super outperforms the standard RTX 2080 and the previous-gen GTX 1080 Ti, plus it delivers the extra benefits that make RTX cards so sought after. <strong>Ray tracing</strong>, the first main feature, isn't as widespread as many people would like it, but it's still available in popular games like Call of Duty: Modern Warfare, Control, Minecraft, and more. And the RTX 2080 Super includes 48 dedicated cores for ray tracing.</p> \n    <p><strong>DLSS 2.0</strong> is perhaps the more impressive feature that comes standard with this GPU. It employs dedicated Tensor cores to run AI rendering in real-time, effectively boosting frame rates while also making frames come out at a much higher resolution. Because ray tracing can be detrimental to performance, DLSS 2.0 is the perfect pairing.</p> \n    <p>The Founders Edition version of the RTX 2080 Super includes 8GB of GDDR6 VRAM and speedy 496GB/s memory bandwidth, plus a boost clock that can hit 1,815MHz. Those are some beefy numbers, but you will need a decent amount of power to run the card in your gaming PC; NVIDIA recommends at least a 650W power supply unit (PSU). This card is compatible with G-Sync monitors, which have the adaptive sync technology to reduce screen tearing. It will also work with any <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/list-all-nvidia-g-sync-compatible-freesync-monitors\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">FreeSync monitors that are \"G-Sync compatible.\"</a> Whether you're looking to game at 4K or 1440p, the RTX 2080 Super remains one of the best graphics cards for a lot of people.</p> \n    <div class=\"rows left collection\"> \n     <h3 class=\"product reco-block\">NVIDIA RTX 2080 Super Founders Edition</h3> \n     <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" title=\"Best Graphics Card 2020: Top GPUs for Gaming\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/nvidia-rtx-2080-super-founders-edition-se-crop-01.png\" /></a></p> \n     <p>With stellar 4K and 1440p performance at price hundreds less than the RTX 2080 Ti, the RTX 2080 Super is our pick for the best overall GPU for your custom gaming PC. Just make sure it's not overkill for your needs.</p> \n     <p><a class=\"norewrite\"><strong>7.</strong> NVIDIA GTX 1660 Super (From $250)</a></li> \n     </ul> \n     <!--sectionbreak--> \n     <p>Want to turn your plain PC into a powerful gaming PC? You'll want to look at investing in one of our picks for the best graphics card. It's responsible for rendering everything you see on-screen, as well as taking workloads off the CPU when powering through calculations. The last thing you want to do when purchasing a new GPU is to waste your money on an older model or one that's not powerful enough to do what you need. You also don't want to overspend.</p> \n     <p>There are several questions you need to ask yourself. What kind of games are you playing? Love low-impact indie titles or well-optimized esport games? Or do you wish to take full advantage of current-gen AAA gaming and want to enjoy the best graphics at a 4K resolution? If the answer is the former, you'll need to think about more affordable graphics cards that don't require advanced components to get the most out of the GPU.</p> \n     <p>As for more demanding games, it's generally down to your budget and what your current PC has in terms of a processor (CPU), RAM, and more. If your PC build is rocking anything less than a recent Intel Core i5 or AMD Ryzen 5 CPU, it's probably not worth forking out on top-of-the-line and most expensive GPU options. You'll most likely experience what is known as a bottleneck, where a separate piece of hardware isn't capable of keeping up with the GPU's ability.</p> \n     <p>For which resolution and frame rate are you shooting? Entry-level budget GPUs are ideal for 1080p (FHD) gaming, mid-range is best for 1440p (QHD) gaming, and the top-tier options are cut out for 4K (UHD). Of course, you can always drop down to a lower resolution with a top-tier GPU just to get better frame rates, or if you don't want to shell out the cash for a 4K gaming monitor.</p> \n     <p>How long would you like the GPU to last? Going with a budget option now is going to save you money, but it won't be relevant as long as a mid- or upper-range GPU. If you don't want to replace the GPU any time soon, you will want to spend a bit more now to ensure you can continue playing games as they're released in the next few years. With all these questions considered, <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fnvidia-geforce-rtx-2080-super-8gb-gddr6-pci-express-3-0-graphics-card-black-silver%252F6361326.p%253FskuId%253D6361326&amp;token=kCGbq6EW\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA's GeForce RTX 2080 Super</a> is our pick for best graphics card because it hits a sweet spot in terms of performance and price. It's nowhere near as costly as the more powerful RTX 2080 Ti, yet it will deliver a smooth 4K gaming experience (or absolutely smoking 1440p experience). If it's not quite what you're looking for, either in terms of price or performance, there are plenty of other great GPU options available.</p> \n     <hr> \n      <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D44583%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.newegg.com%252Fasus-geforce-rtx-2080-ti-rog-strix-rtx2080ti-o11g-gaming%252Fp%252FN82E16814126263&amp;token=pUk7PAZ0\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" title=\"Best Graphics Card 2020: Top GPUs for Gaming\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/asus-rog-strix-gaming-oc-rtx-2080-ti-se-hero-01.png\" /></a></p> \n      <h2 id=\"2080TI\">2. thanks to offering dedicated cores for ray tracing and DLSS 2.0 technologies to help boost your gaming experience. Like the RTX 2080 Super, the 2070 Super has 8GB of GDDR6 VRAM, though its memory is a bit slower, it has fewer CUDA cores, and it doesn't have as high of a clock speed. Still, performance nearly matches that of the standard RTX 2080.</p> \n        <p>If you're in search of a GPU that can deliver a quality 4K experience, the RTX 2080 Super or 2080 Ti are still better choices, though the 2070 Super will allow you to dabble at the higher resolution. Where it really shines, though, is at 1440p. You should be able to max out most modern game settings and still achieve high, smooth frame rates. And thanks to <strong>G-Sync technology</strong>, pairing the GPU up with a compatible monitor will further reduce any screen tearing.</p> \n        <p>The fact that the RTX 2070 Super costs hundreds less again than our top pick no doubt makes it quite appealing to many gamers who just don't have nearly $1,000 to spend on a single piece of hardware in their gaming PC. NVIDIA does recommend at least a 650W PSU to pair with the 2070 Super, so that might be a necessary upgrade. In any case, this is a stellar card for anyone wanting to stick with 1440p and <em>absolutely crush frame rates</em>.</p> \n        <div class=\"rows left collection\"> \n         <h3 class=\"product reco-block\">NVIDIA GeForce RTX 2070 Super Founders Edition</h3> \n         <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" title=\"Best Graphics Card 2020: Top GPUs for Gaming\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2019/07/geforce-rtx-2070-super-shop-d.png\" /></a></p> \n         <p>It costs considerably less than the RTX 2080 Super, yet it can still deliver 4K and 1440p gaming. technology</li> \n            <li>High memory bandwidth compared to RTX 2060</li> \n           </ul> \n           <h3 class=\"cons\">Cons</h3> \n           <ul> \n            <li>Costs more than the AMD RX 5700 XT for lesser performance</li> \n            <li>Ray tracing better paired with beefier GPUs</li> \n           </ul> \n           <p>The <strong>NVIDIA RTX 2060 Super</strong> is a significant upgrade over the standard RTX 2060, and no doubt those who rushed out to buy the original 2060 wish they'd waited for the Super version. Performance-wise it sits somewhere near the standard RTX 2070, meaning it has the power to handle a quality 1440p gaming experience. Most AAA games will be able to be played on high or, in some cases, ultra settings without sacrificing frame rates. And if you're working with a 1080p monitor, this card will deliver a smooth, ultra experience no matter the title.</p> \n           <p>Ray tracing and DLSS 2.0 technologies are included, though if you're really into ray tracing, you still probably want to go with one of the higher-end NVIDIA cards. The 2060 Super will get the job done, but you will sacrifice performance in other areas with it enabled.</p> \n           <p>There's also the matter of cost. AMD's RX 5700 XT, which performs slightly better, won't have you spending as much money. If it's just raw performance you're after and don't mind the lack of extra NVIDIA RTX features, it's probably the better buy. In any case, the RTX 2060 Super remains an attractive card for those on Team Green who are looking for an introductory GPU for ray tracing and high-quality 1440p gaming.</p> \n           <div class=\"rows left collection\"> \n            <h3 class=\"product reco-block\">GIGABYTE Gaming OC RTX 2060 Super</h3> \n            <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" NVIDIA and its extra RTX features should find the RTX 2060 Super to be a solid introductory card for 1080p or 1440p gaming.</p> \n            <p><a It delivers a smooth 1080p performance and doesn't have an unreasonable price.</p> \n            <p><strong>Memory:</strong> 6GB GDDR6 | <strong>Memory bandwidth:</strong> 336GB/s | <strong>Memory \n             <li>NVIDIA Turing architecture</li> \n             <li>G-Sync technology</li> \n             <li>Enough performance for smooth 1080p</li> \n            </ul> \n            <h3 class=\"cons\">Cons</h3> \n            <ul> \n             <li>Not intended for 1440p</li> \n             <li>No DLSS 2.0</li> \n            </ul> \n            <p>Not everyone sees a need to game at a higher resolution than 1080p. Displays are more affordable, and fewer pixels generally allows for a much higher frame rate. If you're not looking to overspend on a GPU, NVIDIA's <strong>GTX 1660 Super</strong> should make a great pick. It's not an RTX card, so it doesn't offer dedicated ray-tracing cores, though a driver update does allow it to technically be compatible. DLSS 2.0 is not supported. It's still based on Turing architecture that makes it relatively power efficient. This GPU also sits atop our list of <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-cheap-graphics-cards\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best cheap graphics cards</a>.</p> \n            <p>It has 6GB of GDDR6 VRAM (the base GTX 1660 uses GDDR5) and rather high memory bandwidth at 336GB/s, allowing it to edge out even the 8GB version of the AMD RX 5500 XT in terms of raw performance. You're going to see elevated, smooth frame rates at 1080p with pretty much any game, even at high settings.</p> \n            <div class=\"rows left collection\"> \n             <h3 class=\"product reco-block\">MSI Gaming X GTX 1660 Super</h3> \n             <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" title=\"Best Graphics Card 2020: Top GPUs for Gaming\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/msi-gaming-x-rtx-1660-super-se-crop-01.png\" /></a></p> \n             <p>The NVIDIA GTX 1660 Super is a perfect card for anyone happy with smooth gaming at 1080p. It doesn't offer RTX benefits like dedicated ray-tracing cores and DLSS 2.0, but it's still a great GPU with reliable performance.</p> \n             <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.anrdoezrs.net%2Flinks%2F100048247%2Ftype%2Fdlg%2Fsid%2FUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%2Fhttps%3A%2F%2Fwww.dell.com%2Fen-us%2Fshop%2Faccessories%2Fapd%2Fab076007&amp;token=rTuYKWFL\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$287 at Dell</a></p> \n             <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fmsi-gaming-x-nvidia-geforce-gtx-1660-super-6gb-gddr6-pci-express-3-0-graphics-card-black-gray%252F6389333.p%253FskuId%253D6389333&amp;token=Kaan83gI\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$265 at Best Buy</a></p> \n             <p class=\"end\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07ZK69HDK/?smid=A1XBPHGHAXLHDG&amp;psc=1&amp;tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44996YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$297 at Amazon</a></p> \n            </div> \n            <hr> \n             <h2>What about all the other graphics cards?</h2> \n             <p>There are a ton of other best graphics cards on the market, ranging from <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-gpus-under-100\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">deep budget sub-$100 options</a>, <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/which-graphics-card-do-you-need-vr\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best graphics cards for VR</a>, <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards-4k-monitors\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best graphics cards for 4K</a>, and on up to professional-grade cards intended for specialized design and development work. But as far as GPUs cut out for gaming go, these are the cards that make the most sense in terms of performance-to-price ratio.</p> \n             <p>Graphics cards are generally available from several different manufacturers; performance and specs are generally the same with just slight differences, though the price, cooling, and overall design will differ. No matter your preferred resolution, preferred games, or preferred manufacturers, you're going to find a GPU in this guide that will suit your next fresh PC build or upgrade.</p> \n             <hr> \n              <h2>Is it a good time to upgrade your graphics card?</h2> \n              <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" title=\"Best Graphics Card 2020: Top GPUs for Gaming\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/nvidia-rtx-30-series.jpg\" /></a></p> \n              <p>With <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/nvidia-unveils-rtx-3090-rtx-3080-rtx-3070-pricing-details-availability\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">NVIDIA's latest RTX 30-series GPUs</a> looming just over the horizon, you probably want to hold off on buying a new card right now, at least unless you get a fantastic deal. A lot of people or undoubtedly looking to offload their old GPUs so that you might find one secondhand at a great price.</p> \n              <p>Just how big of an upgrade are the new RTX 30-series GPUs from NVIDIA? Ampere tech has propelled these GPUs forward in the biggest generational leap, with the RTX 3070 reportedly putting out a better performance than the RTX 2080 Ti. NVIDIA is claiming a price of about $499, which is absolutely nuts considering the price of the 2080 Ti.</p> \n              <p>Stepping up, the RTX 3080 is reportedly twice as fast as the RTX 2080, which will put it firmly in a position to handle 4K at 60 FPS. It's expected to start around $699 for the Founder's Edition.</p> \n              <p>Finally, the beastly RTX 3090 is reportedly 50% faster than the Titan RTX and is designed to handle 8K gaming at 60 FPS. Those are some big numbers, and with that performance comes a price tag somewhere around $1,499.</p> \n              <h2>Do you need to upgrade graphics cards?</h2> \n              <p>Trying to figure out whether or not it's time to upgrade your GPU can be challenging. Of course, if you're seeing signs that your GPU is dying — screen artifacts, PC crashes, whining — it's no doubt time to upgrade. But if your current GPU is working fine, do you really need something new?</p> \n              <p>That depends on what types of games you want to play and at what resolution. If you were satisfied with low-impact indie games and built a PC to handle them, you'll no doubt find that your PC struggles to keep up with a hot new AAA title that snagged your eye. The same goes for resolution. If you're upgrading your monitor from 1080p to 1440p or 4K, a new GPU is likely required to make the most of the higher-resolution display.</p> \n              <p>Whenever a new generation of GPUs is released, the previous generation seems to look disproportionately old. Say, for example, you have an NVIDIA GTX 980 in your PC. It's a great GPU, but it's going to be four generations behind once the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/geforce-rtx-3080-ti-leak-reveals-30-performance-uplift-over-2080-ti\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">RTX 30-series GPUs are released</a>. And that brings up another issue: should you wait until the next generation is released? NVIDIA and AMD are usually tight-lipped when it comes to new hardware, but leaks and rumors will usually indicate that something is coming soon. And if you do indeed have a concrete release date, it's likely best to wait for the new cards to come out.</p> \n              <p>Finally, you don't want to upgrade your GPU if you can't also afford to upgrade the rest of your PC components to keep up. Buying an AMD RX 5700 XT GPU and installing it alongside 8GB of RAM and a 4th Gen Intel Core i5 CPU is not going to allow the GPU to realize its full potential. Plus, you might not have a large enough PSU unit to provide enough power to your system, or the cooling system might not be beefy enough to keep the PC running optimally. Always be sure you can upgrade sufficient to avoid bottlenecking the system.</p> \n              <h2>How to check what PC hardware you already have</h2> \n              <p>Whenever you look at investing in a new component for your PC, it's good practice to run a piece of software to have a gander at what you have already. This will help determine just how recent other components are and whether or not they will become a bottleneck for your upcoming GPU purchase. To have a look at what makes everything tick inside the PC case, there are many software options available; <a href=\"https://www.cpuid.com/softwares/cpu-z.html\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">CPU-Z</a>, and <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.anrdoezrs.net%2Flinks%2F100048247%2Ftype%2Fdlg%2Fsid%2FUUwpUdUnU44996YYr%2Fhttps%3A%2F%2Fwww.piriform.com%2Fspeccy&amp;token=i3j1CF5Y\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Speccy</a> are two we would recommend.</p> \n              <p>These apps will tell you what motherboard you have, as well as CPU, RAM, and other bits and pieces. We'll mainly need to see what CPU you have, and a good measurement to use to determine how good your CPU will be with a new GPU purchase is <a href=\"https://benchmarks.ul.com/compare/best-cpus?redirected=true\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">3DMark</a>. The higher the 3DMark score, the better a CPU generally is in gaming and other intensive applications. It shouldn't be used as a definitive value, but the 3DMark score of a specific chip will give you an idea as to how powerful it is.</p> \n              <p>As well as the score, one should also consider the age of the processor, the generation it's part of, the manufacturing process used, the cooler installed, whether or not it's overclocked, and how many cores you're rocking. Intel has its <a href=\"https://ark.intel.com/content/www/us/en/ark.html\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">ARK platform</a> available for conveniently searching its portfolio of CPUs. If you're on #TeamRed, AMD has a similar feature on its <a href=\"http://products.amd.com/en-us/search?k=DesktopProcessors\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">own website</a>.</p> \n              <h2>How to choose a display resolution for PC gaming</h2> \n              <p>If you're building a new PC from the ground up, you might be wondering for which resolution to aim. There are plenty of <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-gaming-monitors\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">great gaming monitors</a> in 1080p, 1440p, and 4K, so it can be tough to choose. What you need to consider is price, fidelity, and the power of the PC hardware you're interested in including.</p> \n              <p>A 1080p gaming monitor will generally cost the least, but will still include high refresh rate and low response time, both of which are features gamers search out. It's not going to look as crisp as 1440p or 4K, but it will also take quite a bit less power to run games at a high frame rate. You're going to be able to get away with a lower-tier GPU and CPU, saving you more money.</p> \n              <p>Bumping things up to 1440p is going to make everything look better. Once you've made the switch to QHD, dropping back down to 1080p is noticeable. The issue with 1440p, however, is that monitors generally cost more, plus you're going to want beefier hardware to achieve high frame rates. The better the GPU and CPU, the better performance you will see at 1440p. Even the high-end RTX 2070 Super and RX 5700 XT that can dabble with 4K will do much better running with a 1440p display.</p> \n              <p>And finally, we have 4K. It's a rather big jump, even from 1440p, and you should have top-tier hardware to get the most of it. 4K displays are expensive, so buying one and pairing it with a subpar PC is not advised. Even with a high-end GPU and CPU, don't expect frame rates to get anywhere near what you can achieve at 1080p and 1440p.</p> \n              <h2 class=\"no-amazon\">Credits — The team that worked on this guide</h2> \n              <p class=\"credit\"><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" title=\"Best Graphics Card 2020: Top GPUs for Gaming\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/thumbnail/public/field/image/2018/05/cale-hunt-avatar-01.jpg\" /></a></p> \n              <p class=\"end\"><strong>Cale Hunt</strong> is a staff writer at Windows Central. /2020/07/sapphire-pulse-rx-5600-xt-se-hero-01.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn32@2020_6/2020/09/05/08-44-16-536_170723da5734740f.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/sapphire-pulse-rx-5600-xt-se-crop-01.png":null,"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/gigabyte-gaming-oc-rtx-2060-super-se-hero-01.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn39@2020_6/2020/09/05/08-44-19-665_d7dbff08d1e64e97.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/gigabyte-gaming-oc-rtx-2060-super-se-crop-01.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn44@2020_6/2020/09/05/08-44-14-406_09de91c14f456831.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/msi-gaming-x-gtx-1660-super-se-hero-01.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn43@2020_6/2020/09/05/08-44-16-689_fcbb793efbf3907d.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/msi-gaming-x-rtx-1660-super-se-crop-01.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn88@2020_3/2020/09/05/08-44-15-510_3878051501883464.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/nvidia-rtx-30-series.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn56@2020_5/2020/09/05/08-44-16-144_ceef1fab1ac021e7.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/thumbnail/public/field/image/2018/05/cale-hunt-avatar-01.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn48@2020_2/2020/09/05/08-44-16-750_f7406ca1c95b0b45.webp","https://passport.mobilenations.com/avatars/000/001/025/1025269.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn73@2020_5/2020/09/05/08-44-17-733_470789f048b02052.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/wmexperts/~4/44JGrw-4ZQo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn68@2020_3/2020/09/05/08-44-14-295_886879f05f527582.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1599295452318},{"createdTime":"2020-09-05 16:44:12","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:44:12","title":"Apple vs. Epic and how it rekindled a love of open source software","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/f--hDBYzKeo/apple-vs-epic-made-me-explore-open-source-software","description":"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/apple-vs-epic-made-me-explore-open-source-software\" title=\"The Apple vs. Epic saga put me on the path to open source\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/field/image/2020/09/iphone-xr-fortnite.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"intro\">The Epic Games vs. Apple war highlights how you can't really rely on any of the big tech firms. And it prompted me to go looking once more at open-source software.</p>\n\n<p>The <a href=\"https://www.imore.com/apple-responds-judges-temporary-order-lawsuit-against-epic-games\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Epic Games vs. Apple saga</a> is well storied already so that I won't be going over old ground here. But the whole sorry tale did prompt me to rethink how I use my tech, both for work and for personal use. Because big tech companies can burn you, and often do.</p>\n\n<p>I'm not really a Fortnite player, so the loss of access on iOS doesn't really affect me, but not being able to use xCloud on there certainly does. All of these big companies have their ecosystem plays, and it seems you're not entirely safe locking into any of them.</p>\n\n<p>And while it's impossible to avoid in many cases, there's plenty of software out there that doesn't rely on the shackles of Apple, Google, Microsoft, Facebook, Amazon, and so on. Free and open-source software (FOSS) doesn't just come without a price tag; it comes free of any required attachments to a big ecosystem, and in probably more cases than you think, it can change the way you use a PC.</p>\n\n<h2>Big tech cancels or changes products at its user's cost</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/apple-vs-epic-made-me-explore-open-source-software\" title=\"The Apple vs. Epic saga put me on the path to open source\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/field/image/2016/09/hp-elite-x3-hero-window.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Remember Windows Phone? The biggest example of a tech cancellation in recent memory for regulars to this site, but it's proof of how big things can get when it comes to pulling the rug out from under the users, from under us. By contrast, Android is open source, so even if Google, for some reason, decided to stop making a phone OS, someone else would likely pick up the reigns. Indeed custom versions have been a thing since pretty much the beginning.</p>\n\n<p>It isn't quite the same as what's going on between Epic and Apple, of course, but its impact was very similar. A bunch of people who relied on this thing being around then had to start looking elsewhere. Had Microsoft open-sourced Windows for phones, I guarantee there would be a community still building and supporting devices.</p>\n\n<blockquote class=\"pull right\">\n  <p>These companies all make changes or closures, and it's you and I that suffer for it.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>But it happens on a smaller scale, too. Most recently, Apple acquired Dark Sky and has since shut down its Android app, and the API will cease to function from the end of next year. Affecting users and affecting developers, both of which will have to transition to something else.</p>\n\n<p>Facebook recently announced that Oculus owners will be forced to login with a Facebook account soon. And some of us never got over the closure of Google Reader. Even today.</p>\n\n<p>All different examples, but there's a common theme. All of these ecosystem plays come at a cost. All the big tech companies want, no, need to lock you in to continue a steady source of revenue, but it's not necessarily in your best interests.</p>\n\n<h2>FOSS doesn't just mean Linux</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/apple-vs-epic-made-me-explore-open-source-software\" title=\"The Apple vs. Epic saga put me on the path to open source\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2019/05/gimp.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>The part of the Epic vs. Apple argument I agree with the most is that there's no alternative on iOS to buying apps. No alternative means no competition, which means Apple can keep charging developers 30%, and the users of the platform ultimately pay the price.</p>\n\n<p>Android, of course, is a little more open, with alternatives to acquire apps that don't involve Google, such as Samsung's own store, the Amazon Appstore, and of course, Huawei's AppGallery since they don't even have access to Google. But there are options out there.</p>\n\n<p>Options are what you get with FOSS. And it doesn't mean you have to use Linux. Open-source software is prevalent across Windows, Mac, and Linux, as well as mobile and the web. I've been dabbling more recently with Linux and Chrome OS alongside my regular Windows 10 use. I have already found several amazing applications that work on all those platforms that are capable of replacing software I've been using for years.</p>\n\n<h2>Open source apps can be amazing</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/apple-vs-epic-made-me-explore-open-source-software\" title=\"The Apple vs. Epic saga put me on the path to open source\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/vs-code-chromebook-install7.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Many years ago, I used <a href=\"https://www.gimp.org/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">GIMP</a>, a popular cross-platform open-source image editor along the lines of Photoshop. Then, for reasons I can't really understand, I moved to paying for an Adobe CC subscription. Now I'm back on GIMP, or more specifically, a forked version called <a href=\"https://glimpse-editor.github.io/#:~:text=Glimpse%20Image%20Editor,use%20of%20free%2Flibre%20software.\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Glimpse</a>. This is an incredibly impressive piece of software with plugins galore available, supporting Windows, Mac, and Linux and costing absolutely nothing. No subscription to Adobe, just great software built by people who just want to make it as good as it can be. Video editors would do well to check out the impressive <a href=\"https://kdenlive.org/en/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">KDenLive</a>, which can also be used on all the major platforms as an alternative to Adobe Premiere.</p>\n\n<p>It doesn't stop there, either. Microsoft 365 is a great package, but if all you want is something lighter, free, and compatible with Office files, there are suites like <a href=\"https://www.libreoffice.org/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">LibreOffice</a>. Once again, this is available on all the major platforms, completely free and open source.  Microsoft has been contributing more to the open-source community of late, too, with one example being its <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/how-install-microsoft-visual-studio-code-chromebook\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Visual Studio Code</a> application. A personal favorite is <a href=\"https://stackedit.io/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">StackEdit</a>, a web-based open-source markdown editor which has become my new place for writing all my work.</p>\n\n<p>And did you know that the Telegram app is open source? It's also a much better service than WhatsApp and can be used on many platforms all at once.</p>\n\n<h2>The future is open source</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/apple-vs-epic-made-me-explore-open-source-software\" title=\"The Apple vs. Epic saga put me on the path to open source\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/kdenlive-screen.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Obviously, there will always be ecosystem tie ins and places you're unable to avoid \"the man.\" Gaming is a big one, of course, and content. But in those cases, you should always keep your options open. If you buy all your content in Microsoft's store, then what happens if, as has happened in the past, Microsoft decides to pull the plug?</p>\n\n<p>I'm hardly an expert; I'm only just beginning to find my feet in the world of open-source software. But this whole debacle where one enormous company has stopped another enormous company using its services because it wants to keep more money for itself shines a golden glow on the FOSS community.</p>\n\n<p>These folks are making good software for the sole purpose of making good software. If you choose to toss a few bucks their way to help cover costs and keep the development train rolling, that's great; I've done that regularly.</p>\n\n<p>The issue isn't things costing money, I'm happy to pay, and I'm happy to donate to developers offering a free product to help them keep doing good work. The issue is when big business decisions start affecting the little guy. Us. I want to use the software I know was built for the sole purpose of being a good piece of software, not to lock me into a subscription or keep me using one particular platform. It's refreshing, and it's been a real eye-opener starting to explore what's out there.</p>\n\n<p>Likewise, if you're already a fan of some great open source software, share it with us in the comments below so we can all appreciate it.</p></div></div></div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/wmexperts/~4/f--hDBYzKeo\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\"
