<div class=\"field-items\">\n  <div class=\"field-item even\">\n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-9.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p class=\"intro\">How Microsoft's new Surface Duo foldable functions, and the six \"postures\" highlighting ways to use the device to its fullest.</p> \n   <p>The <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Microsoft Surface Duo</a> pioneers a new form factor for Android devices, defined by its dual displays and bound by a 360-degree hinge. The slimline design touts versatility, with the company hoping to deliver a new approach to mobile productivity. But the convergence of hardware and software remains crucial to that promise, enabling a variety of scenarios, which Microsoft describes as \"postures.\"</p> \n   <p>Postures on Surface Duo relate to both the physical hardware positioning and the on-screen experience. It launches alongside six predefined postures, adapting to how the user poses, orients, and operates the device.</p> \n   <p>Surface Duo provides a glimpse into how Microsoft is approaching foldables creatively, augmenting the Android operating system with in-house tweaks. The result looks to contextually respond to your workflow, adapting content for the twin-screen setup. Below is every Microsoft Surface Duo posture and how it works.</p> \n   <!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Preorder today</h3> \n   <h4 class=\"product\">Microsoft Surface Duo</h4> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-reco1.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU80067YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fsurface%252Fdevices%252Fsurface-duo&amp;token=sB15QR6F\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at Microsoft</a> <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU80067YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fmicrosoft-surface-duo-128gb-unlocked%252F6419335.p%253FskuId%253D6419335&amp;token=8Oks0KFm\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at Best Buy</a> <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.anrdoezrs.net%2Flinks%2F100048247%2Ftype%2Fdlg%2Fsid%2FUUwpUdUnU80067YYr%2Fhttps%3A%2F%2Fwww.att.com%2Fbuy%2Fphones%2Fmicrosoft-surface-duo-128gb-glacier.html&amp;token=_XamA1i8\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at AT&amp;T</a></p> \n   <p class=\"subtitle\">Two screens are better than one</p> \n   <p class=\"end\">Microsoft delves into the future of foldables with an ambitious dual-screen device, featuring two ultra-thin 5.6-inch AMOLED displays bound by a 360-degree hinge. This pocketable inking-enabled Android smartphone marks the latest in the Surface lineup, geared for mobile productivity.</p> \n   <!-- END RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <nav class=\"article-nav-menu nav\"> \n    <h3>Jump to:</h3> \n    <ul class=\"jumplist col2\"> \n     <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/hLUrODd_e7I/surface-duo-postures#bookmode\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Book Mode</a></li> \n     <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/hLUrODd_e7I/surface-duo-postures#composemode\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Compose Mode</a></li> \n     <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/hLUrODd_e7I/surface-duo-postures#duallandscapemode\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Dual Landscape Mode</a></li> \n     <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/hLUrODd_e7I/surface-duo-postures#singlescreenmode\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Single Screen Mode</a></li> \n     <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/hLUrODd_e7I/surface-duo-postures#tentmode\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Tent Mode</a></li> \n     <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/hLUrODd_e7I/surface-duo-postures#peekmode\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Peek Mode</a></li> \n    </ul> \n   </nav> \n   <h2 id=\"bookmode\">Book Mode: <em>Double the apps at once</em></h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-hand-vertical-hand.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>One of the best showcases for Microsoft Surface Duo's dual-screen form factor is \"Book Mode,\" assuming a book-like posture, with adjacent portrait screens. The setup evokes an experience akin to a traditional paperback, ideal for reading, scrolling, and consuming content across the twin displays.</p> \n   <p>It's the natural posture after opening the device, ideal for experiencing two separate apps side-by-side. It also supports apps optimized for its dual-screen \"spanning\" feature, with content and menus contextually spread across. Third-party apps like Amazon Kindle also explore their own interpretation, emulating the layout of your favorite novels.</p> \n   <p><strong>Best for: Using two apps simultaneously, reading, notes, and documents.</strong></p> \n   <h2 id=\"composemode\">Compose Mode: <em>Laptop in your pocket</em></h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-pen-horizontal.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Compose Mode means rotating the Surface Duo onto its side, using its virtual keyboard to get things done. The posture looks to deliver an ultra-portable laptop alternative, with a full-screen typing experience for added immersion. You enter this form by orienting the device, which pushes the app up top, with the keyboard docked below.</p> \n   <p>Extending the virtual keyboard to landscape triggers it to occupy the full 5.6-inch screen, suited for cranking out longer emails or working on documents. The device uses a dual-screen spin on Microsoft SwiftKey, which includes tweaks like a split keyboard for added ergonomics. It's the most robust typing experience available on Duo, akin to a mini PC.</p> \n   <p><strong>Best for: Writing longer emails, documents, and general typing.</strong></p> \n   <h2 id=\"duallandscapemode\">Dual Landscape Mode: <em>Full screen experience</em></h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/surface-duo-pinterest.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Microsoft Surface Duo also allows for spanning one experience across both displays, delivering what the company describes as \"Dual Landscape Mode.\" The feature lets apps bridge the full 8.1-inches of the screens when spanned, providing a space to view content on a larger scale.</p> \n   <p>Dual Landscape Mode works with various apps, ideal for viewing long webpages or endless scrolling feeds. Microsoft has shown off the mode with apps like Pinterest and Instagram, where a feed of visual content pops across the twin panels. Looking past the hinge may be a struggle for some, but leverages the entire screen real estate at its best.</p> \n   <p><strong>Best for: Web pages, social media, and viewing other content.</strong></p> \n   <h2 id=\"singlescreenmode\">Single Screen Mode: <em>Back to basics</em></h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-hand.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Microsoft's dual-screen design also includes a 360-degree hinge, allowing one to swing behind the other. Putting the displays back-to-back transforms the device into a usual single-screen phone, confining the experience to just one panel, and improving one-handed usability.</p> \n   <p>The single-screen mode may cut the Surface Duo's defining features but remains crucial to some interactions. Typing one-handed and taking a phone call is near-impossible when wrangling both screens, making this simple posture valuable in everyday usage.</p> \n   <p>The single-screen mode also plays a crucial role in the Surface Duo camera setup, limited to a single 11MP front-facing shooter. The more restricted configuration allows you to reorient its camera, overcoming the need for a rear sensor. The compromise comes from its ultra-thin design, with this handy trick ensuring flexibility for selfies or landscape shots.</p> \n   <p><strong>Best for: Camera, phone calls, one-handed use.</strong></p> \n   <h2 id=\"tentmode\">Tent Mode: <em>Hassle-free video calls and entertainment</em></h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/surface-duo-tent.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>This aptly-named mode leverages the hinged design, allowing you to prop up the Surface Duo in a v-shaped posture. Tent Mode best suits hands-off experiences, angling the display without a separate stand for, or tight grip on, the device.</p> \n   <p>This works well for entertainment, accommodating video apps like YouTube or Netflix in landscape orientation, or cloud gaming like Project xCloud. Video conferencing apps like Microsoft Teams or Zoom also fit, positioning the front-facing camera to keep you in-frame. You can also use it to share content, pulling up documents for friends or clients in-person.</p> \n   <p><strong>Best for: Video playback and conferencing.</strong></p> \n   <h2 id=\"peekmode\">Peek Mode: <em>Check your notifications</em></h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-peek.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>When the Surface Duo is locked and partially open, the device enters what Microsoft describes as \"Peek Mode.\" The feature serves a thin vertical bar down the right-hand side of the display, rounding up the time, app notifications, and other key status icons at a glance. To activate, steadily open your device until the white-on-black preview appears.</p> \n   <p>Peek Mode integrates with Android to serve up system notifications without committing to fully opening the device. It's the company's solution to no outward-facing display, compiling events of interest into an easily consumable panel, instead. It might not be as convenient as an external display but provides the next best solution with the hardware.</p> \n   <p><strong>Best for: Quickly viewing notifications and time.</strong></p> \n   <p>Understanding the Surface Duo's postures provides a glimpse into best using its dual-screen setup. While it's only the foundations of the refreshed Android experience, Microsoft proposes some novel concepts with its modern mobile form factor. In the meantime, Surface Duo preorders are live via the Microsoft Store, starting at $1,399 in the U.S.</p> \n   <!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Preorder today</h3> \n   <h4 class=\"product\">Microsoft Surface Duo</h4> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-postures\" title=\"Surface Duo postures: Every bend and fold you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-reco1.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU80067YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fsurface%252Fdevices%252Fsurface-duo&amp;token=sB15QR6F\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at Microsoft</a> <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU80067YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fmicrosoft-surface-duo-128gb-unlocked%252F6419335.p%253FskuId%253D6419335&amp;token=8Oks0KFm\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at Best Buy</a> <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.anrdoezrs.net%2Flinks%2F100048247%2Ftype%2Fdlg%2Fsid%2FUUwpUdUnU80067YYr%2Fhttps%3A%2F%2Fwww.att.com%2Fbuy%2Fphones%2Fmicrosoft-surface-duo-128gb-glacier.html&amp;token=_XamA1i8\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at AT&amp;T</a></p> \n   <p class=\"subtitle\">Two screens are better than one</p> \n   <p class=\"end\">Microsoft delves into the future of foldables with an ambitious dual-screen device, featuring two ultra-thin 5.6-inch AMOLED displays bound by a 360-degree hinge. field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p class=\"intro\">Adobe Flash Player is approaching its final fall of the curtain.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-outlines-end-support-adobe-flash-player\" title=\"Microsoft outlines end of support for Adobe Flash Player\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_blw/public/field/image/2020/01/microsoft-edge-2020.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<h2 class=\"aside news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>Microsoft outlines the end of support for Adobe Flash Player in a new blog post.</li>\n<li>Microsoft's browser will end support for Adobe Flash Player at the end of 2020.</li>\n<li>Adobe Flash Player is being replaced by more secure technologies.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Microsoft shared an update today on the end of support for Adobe Flash Player. Microsoft already announced that support for Adobe Flash Player would end in December 2020, but a <a href=\"https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2020/09/04/update-adobe-flash-end-support/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">new blog post</a> from the company outlines how enterprise users can get continued support. It also provides a more exact timeline of how support will end.</p>\n\n<p>Adobe Flash Player is less secure than alternatives such as HTML5, WebGL, and WebAssembly. Both the legacy version of Microsoft Edge and the new Microsoft Edge will lose support for Adobe Flash Player at the end of 2020. Additionally, Internet Explorer 11 will lose Adobe Flash support at the end of the year.</p>\n\n<p>While many sites have already migrated away from Adobe Flash Player, some enterprises still rely on it. Enterprise customers can contact Adobe's official partner, <a href=\"https://services.harman.com/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">HARMAN</a>, if they still need support for Adobe Flash Player beyond the end of 2020. Adobe discusses this further in a <a href=\"https://blog.adobe.com/en/fpost/2020/update-for-enterprise-adobe-flash-player.html#gs.f9wrap\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">blog post</a>.</p>\n\n<p>Microsoft will remove all APIs, group policies, and user interfaces that \"specifically govern the behavior of Adobe Flash Player\" from Microsoft Edge (legacy) and Internet Explorer 11 through a Cumulative Update in the summer of 2021, as outlined in its blog post.</p></div></div></div><img +0000","feedId":13006,"bgimg":"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/03/witcher-3-sunset-image.jpg","linkMd5":"16eb727a51131ae0819e576465da34e1","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn72@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-44-12-557_054f1b1441e9ad8f.webp","destWidth":800,"destHeight":450,"sourceBytes":50066,"destBytes":50066,"author":"Sean Endicott","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/03/witcher-3-sunset-image.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn72@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-44-12-557_054f1b1441e9ad8f.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2019/10/the-witcher-3-box-art.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn52@2020_2/2020/09/05/08-44-14-351_94cf9b4544b73905.webp","https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2019/12/steam-gift-card-50.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn4@2020_5/2020/09/05/08-44-17-723_41301d5523b1de40.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/wmexperts/~4/xhVIUfWJiXU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn60@2020_1/2020/09/05/08-44-18-361_8d8099b18973d0dd.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1599295452302},{"createdTime":"2020-09-05 16:44:12","updatedTime":"2020-09-05 16:44:12","title":"Review: EPOS GSP 602 is now the best gaming headset in my house","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/k4oWtA2RxZM/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review","description":"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p class=\"intro\">A genuinely premium wired gaming headset.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review\" title=\"EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset review: My new go-to gaming headset\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/epos_602_gaming_headset_microphone.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>In an effort to offer a great suite of versatile gaming headsets, Sennheiser has officially rebranded its gaming series as EPOS. Sennheiser aims to bring its legacy of audio expertise to the gaming space with a wide range of purposely designed headsets. This smart business move now gives consumers a more clear distinction between the company's studio focused equipment and gaming accessories.</p>\n\n<p>I was fortunate enough to spend some time with the latest addition to this line — the EPOS 602 Gaming Headset. As someone who typically prefers wired headsets, I was very excited to test out one of the more premium offerings from the EPOS line. Immediatelly upon opening the packaging, it became clear the EPOS 602 was built with quality in mind. After hours of use and several extended gaming sessions, it's safe to say I have finally found my new go-to gaming headset.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Crystal clear audio and pillowy comfort</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">EPOS GSP 602</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review\" title=\"EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset review: My new go-to gaming headset\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/epos_gsp_602_gaming_headset.png\"></a></p>\n\n<p>\n<span itemprop=\"reviewRating\" itemscope itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Rating\" class=\"article-rating article-rating--inline app-none\">\n  <span class=\"article-rating-stars\">\n                  \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar-half\"></span>\n      </span>  <meta itemprop=\"bestRating\" content=\"5.0\">\n  <meta itemprop=\"worstRating\" content=\"0.0\">\n  <meta itemprop=\"ratingValue\" content=\"4.5\">\n</span>\n\n</p>\n\n<p><strong>Bottom line</strong>: The EPOS GSP 602 is now the best gaming headset in my home. However, this quality certainly comes with a price tag that might be a bit hefty for some folks.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Incredible hi-fi audio quality</li>\n<li>Closed acoustics offer great noise canceling  </li>\n<li>Pillowy comfort  </li>\n<li>Versatile connectivity  </li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Price is a bit steep</li>\n<li>Gap in cushion band was occasionally uncomfortable</li>\n<li>Lack of extreme low-end may disappoint some </li>\n</ul>\n\n<p class=\"end\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/EPOS-Sennheiser-GSP-602-Noise-Cancelling/dp/B08DFXYB2T/ref=sr_1_3?dchild=1&#38;keywords=gsp+602&#38;qid=1599068710&#38;sr=8-3&#38;mnsid=linkomatic&#38;tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=linkomatic\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$219 at Amazon</a></p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2>How is the EPOS GSP 602's <em>sound</em> quality? </h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review\" title=\"EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset review: My new go-to gaming headset\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/epos_gsp_602_gaming_headset_top_down.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<table class=\"spec-table right\">\n<thead>\n<tr>\n  <th>Category</th>\n  <th>GameNameXXX</th>\n</tr>\n</thead>\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n  <td>Compatability</td>\n  <td>PC (Wired - 2x3.5mm) Consoles (Wired - 3.5mm) Mobile (Wired - 3.5mm)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n  <td>Frequency Response</td>\n  <td>10Hz - 30kHz</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n  <td>Design</td>\n  <td>Over-Ear (Closed Acoustic)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n  <td>Mic Frequency Response</td>\n  <td>10Hz - 18kHz</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n  <td>Cable Length</td>\n  <td>2.5m (PC) 1.2m (Console/Mobile)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n  <td>Connector Plugs</td>\n  <td>2 x 3.5 mm (3-pole connectors) 1 x 3.5 mm (4-pole connectors)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n  <td>Price</td>\n  <td>$219</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n  <td>Weight</td>\n  <td>395g</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody>\n</table>\n\n<p>In a previous review, I praised the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sennheiser-gsp-300-gaming-headset-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Sennheiser GSP 300 Gaming Headset</a> for its amazing sound quality and clear, high-quality drivers. The EPOS GSP 602 delivers notably better audio thanks to some incredible hi-fi drivers with a range of 10-30,000Hz, whereas the GSP 300 sat at a respectable, but inferior 15-26,000Hz. This noticeable superior extended frequency response range maintained audio clarity even during the most intense action sequences. High-end focused sounds like glass shattering or metallic scraping were bright and distinct, and low-end centric noises like roars or footsteps were present and pronounced.</p>\n\n<p>While replaying the campaign for Gears 5, the character's voices were never lost in the cacophonous wall of constant explosions, which is something I had experienced with previous bass-heavy headsets. If you are accustomed to extremely boosted low-end headsets however, you may be disappointed as those same explosions from Gears 5 lacked the concussive impact of my <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/hyperx-cloud-alpha-headset-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">HyperX Cloud Alphas</a>.</p>\n\n<p>As somewhat of an audio purist, I appreciated the GSP 602's focus on natural audio quality without artificial boosts to sub-bass frequencies. The closed-acoustic design also does a remarkable job of naturally isolating background noise. Even without active noise cancelation, I was able to get fully immersed in my gaming experiences thanks to Sennheiser's expertise in this area.</p>\n\n<h2>What I like about the EPOS GSP 602 <em>design</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review\" title=\"EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset review: My new go-to gaming headset\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/epos_602_gaming_headset_volume_knob.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>The GSP 602 strikes the perfect design balance between modern, flashy gaming headsets and sleek minimalism. The deep blue color and vivid orange cushions add personality without diving headfirst into the gaudy cliches of many modern gaming headset manufacturers. Subtle, sharp edges, and splashes of a matte metallic finish give it a very premium look and feel. A sizeable volume control knob on the right side of the headset and an adjustable microphone arm on the left side keeps all controls contained to the headset itself.</p>\n\n<p>I also found the fairly sleek frame very reminiscent of something a pilot might wear, so there's some great roleplay potential for all the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-flight-simulator-xbox\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Flight Simulator</a> fans out there. For folks who maybe aren't as excited about the orange and blue color scheme of the GSP 602, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/EPOS-Sennheiser-GSP-602-Noise-Cancelling/dp/B08DFXYB2T/ref=sr_1_3?dchild=1&#38;keywords=gsp+602&#38;qid=1599068710&#38;sr=8-3&#38;mnsid=linkomatic&#38;tag=wpcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=linkomatic\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">EPOS GSP 600</a> is the same great headset in a more neutral black with red option.</p>\n\n<h2>How <em>comfortable</em> is the EPOS GSP 602?</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review\" title=\"EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset review: My new go-to gaming headset\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/epos_602_gaming_headset_side.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>In regards to comfort and overall feel, the GSP 602 is an absolute win. The faux-leather ear cushions are thick and cozy. Wearing this headset is like pressing two mini memory foam pillows on either side of your face. The openings for these cushions are also incredibly large, allowing your entire ear to be surrounded. This huge design perk kept the headset feeling great even during lengthy grind sessions in <a href=\"https://www.imore.com/final-fantasy-crystal-chronicles-remastered-edition-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Final Fantasy Crystal Chronicles: Remastered</a>.</p>\n\n<p>There's also a fairly dense strip of cushion along the top of the headband, delivering even more sustained comfort. The only issue I ran in to with the band, and really the comfort of the GSP 602 in general, was a gap in the center of the foam, which sometimes pressed my hair in the wrong direction creating the sore \"hat-hair\" sensation, but to be fair I have a pretty massive head compared to the average person, so that could be more of an isolated issue.</p>\n\n<h2>How is the <em>microphone</em> quality on the EPOS GSP 602?</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review\" title=\"EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset review: My new go-to gaming headset\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/epos_602_gaming_headset_head_on.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>As a low-key audiophile, my expectations for gaming headset microphones are always very low. That being said, I was remarkably surprised by the clarity delivered by the microphone of the GSP 602. It's a massive improvement over the GSP 300 in almost every way and even competes with the shockingly solid performance of the HyperX Cloud II.</p>\n\n<p>There is not much to report in regards to the extreme high or low end here, but doing side by side tests in an Xbox Party chat, my friend group all seemed to agree that of the GSP 300, GSP 602, and HyperX Cloud Alpha, the GSP 602 had the clearest microphone quality. It wasn't able to deliver the same low-end presence of the Cloud Alphas, but during action-oriented multiplayer sessions, that low-end response just gets lost in the chaos anyway. As someone who frequently plays communication-focused PVP games like Gears 5, Smite, and Bleeding Edge, mic clarity is very important and I'm happy to report that the GSP 602 beautifully delivered in this regard.</p>\n\n<p>There's also a clever mute-toggle linked to the arm microphone that offers an obvious indicator for whether or not your mic is muted. Just remember to lower that arm before delivering any crucial in-game battle plans.</p>\n\n<h2>How <em>compatible</em> is this headset?</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/epos-gsp-602-gaming-headset-review\" title=\"EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset review: My new go-to gaming headset\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/09/epos_602_gaming_headset_profile.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Far and away my biggest critiques of previous models in Sennheiser's gaming headset series have been odd and clunky cable solutions. Thankfully, the team at EPOS has made enormous strides in this department with the GSP 602. The headset includes two completely detachable 2.5mm to 3.5mm cables — one with a single 3.5mm jack for consoles or mobile devices and a second with a dual 3.5mm connectors for PC gaming.</p>\n\n<p>These versatile cable options have made this my new defacto headset for gaming on any of my devices. I've been able to fairly seamlessly use this on my PC, Xbox One X, Nintendo Switch, and even just for listening to music on my phone. The included audio cables are high quality, woven-fiber with respectable lengths for basically any use case. If you're looking for a great all-in-one gaming headset, the EPOS GSP 602 can confidently fill that role.</p>\n\n<h2>Bottom line: Should you buy the EPOS GSP 602 Gaming Headset?</h2>\n\n<p>With a background in studio audio production earlier on in life, I've been fairly spoiled when it comes to headsets. In the gaming space, I've found myself frustrated because many gaming-oriented headsets producers focus on bright gimmicks and tacky buzzwords to market their products to a younger audience. While Sennheiser is officially releasing these products under the EPOS banner, the 70 years of experience in studio-quality audio equipment remains intact with the GSP 602.</p>\n\n<p>    </p><div itemprop=\"reviewRating\" itemscope itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Rating\" class=\"article-rating article-rating--full app-none\">\n    <span class=\"article-rating-score\">4.5</span>\n    <span class=\"article-rating-outof\">out of 5</span>\n    <span class=\"article-rating-stars\">\n                  \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar\"></span>\n                    \n    <span class=\"article-rating-star fa fa-customstar-half\"></span>\n      </span>    <meta itemprop=\"bestRating\" content=\"5.0\">\n    <meta itemprop=\"worstRating\" content=\"0.0\">\n    <meta itemprop=\"ratingValue\" content=\"4.5\">\n  </div>\n\n\n<p>This headset delivers crystal clear audio, pillowy comfort, extreme versatility, and a minimalistic design I absolutely love. All of these great features do come with a hefty price tag however and this will ultimately be the biggest deciding factor for many customers. At around $220, this is certainly a premium wired headset, but the beautifully crafted headset EPOS GSP 602 now stands proudly as the best gaming headset in my house.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$219 at Amazon</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">An absolutely standout gaming headset</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">For folks who are in the market for a quality gaming headset and have the money to spend, the GSP 602 is worth every penny.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK --></div></div></div><img field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p class=\"intro\">HONOR's latest laptop features a large screen as its biggest draw.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/honor-announce-magicbook-pro\" title=\"HONOR's MagicBook Pro packs a big screen into a little body\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>HONOR announced the MagicBook Pro laptop today at IFA 2020.</li>\n<li>The laptop features an AMD Ryzen 5 and integrated Radeon graphics.</li>\n<li>The MagicBook Pro will be available from September 7, 2020 starting at €899.9.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>HONOR announced the <a href=\"https://www.hihonor.com/germany/product/honor-magicbook-pro\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">MagicBook Pro</a> today during its IFA 2020 event. The laptop features a large 16.1-inch screen packed into a smaller form factor. The MagicBook Pro will be available from September 7, 2020 starting at €899.9. HONOR did not discuss any launch of the laptop in the United States.</p>\n\n<p>The new laptop from HONOR runs on an AMD Ryzen 5 4600H processor and features a 16.1-inch display with a 90 percent screen-to-body ratio. It pairs that processor with integrated Radeon graphics with six cores and 12 threads. The display of the laptop has 100 percent sRGB and reaches 300 nits of brightness.</p>\n\n<p>Inside, the laptop has dual fans and dual heat pipes to stay cool. HONOR highlights that its design within the MagicBook 14 Pro delivers 20 percent more airflow than traditional cooling fans.</p>\n\n<div class=\"media-gallery-wrap\"><div compact form factor. The laptop has a 16.1-inch screen despite having a similar footprint to many 15-inch laptops, and it is 16.9mm thin.</p></div></div></div><img field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-preorder-where-buy\" title=\"Surface Duo preorders: Price, release date, and where to buy\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-hero-pen-surface-earbuds.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"intro\">Microsoft's dual-screen Surface Duo launches September, and we have all the details on preorders, pricing, and where to buy.</p>\n\n<p>The <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Microsoft Surface Duo</a> launches this September, marking a return ahead of schedule for the experimental foldable device. The company returns to the smartphone space with a dual-screen flagship, retaining many existing Surface family signatures, while embracing Android for the first time. You may have some questions, and we have all the answers.</p>\n\n<p>Here's what you need to know about Surface Duo preorders, including its release date, price, and where you'll be able to buy it.</p>\n\n<h2 id=\"preorders\" class=\"separator\">Microsoft Surface Duo preorders now live</h2>\n\n<p>Microsoft Surface Duo is now available for preorder in the U.S. ahead of its formal release date scheduled for September 10, 2020. The ambitious foldable device arrives through three partnered retailers across the nation, with a $1,400 retail price for its entry-level, unlocked model. It will also be available via online retailers, and on physical store shelves, after release.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Preorders Live</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Microsoft Surface Duo</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-preorder-where-buy\" title=\"Surface Duo preorders: Price, release date, and where to buy\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-reco1.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU79409YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fsurface%252Fdevices%252Fsurface-duo&#38;token=99bVNscz\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at Microsoft</a>\n<a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU79409YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fmicrosoft-surface-duo-128gb-unlocked%252F6419335.p%253FskuId%253D6419335&#38;token=YP1FIkaF\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $1,400 at Best Buy</a>\n<a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.anrdoezrs.net%2Flinks%2F100048247%2Ftype%2Fdlg%2Fsid%2FUUwpUdUnU79409YYr%2Fhttps%3A%2F%2Fwww.att.com%2Fbuy%2Fphones%2Fmicrosoft-surface-duo-128gb-glacier.html&#38;token=r1i9GcJ9\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">From $47/mo at AT&#38;T</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Two screens are better than one.</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Microsoft delves into the future of foldables with an ambitious dual-screen device, featuring two ultra-thin 5.6-inch AMOLED displays bound by a 360-degree hinge. This pocketable inking-enabled Android smartphone marks the latest in the Surface lineup, geared for mobile productivity.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<p>Microsoft Store, Best Buy, and AT&#38;T preorders are now live in the U.S.</p>\n\n<p>Featuring two 5.6-inch AMOLED displays, 1800x1350 (401 PPI) resolution, and a 360-degree hinge, the Microsoft Surface Duo rides on its dual-screen form factor. The <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-specs-camera-ram-storage-soc-battery\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">final hardware specifications</a> include the Snapdragon 855 processor, 6GB RAM, and up to 256GB storage, which shapes up to be decent, albeit slightly dated. The device also has an 11MP camera, with its hinged design allowing the single sensor to serve as the front- and rear-facing shooter.</p>\n\n<p>One of the best attributes of the Microsoft Surface Duo comes from dual, hinged displays — just 4.8mm each. That's only just thick enough to fit its USB-C port, making an ultra-thin foldable that's easily pocketable when just 9.6mm when closed. Microsoft has also baked in inking for notetaking and sketching, with support for Surface-branded pens out of the box.</p>\n\n<p>But the Surface Duo does have some well-documented limitations, namely forgoing wireless charging, NFC, and 5G support. That helps drive down the cost, even if many features are commonplace on other premium flagships.</p>\n\n<h2>Where to buy the Surface Duo Pen</h2>\n\n<p>With the Surface Duo also boasting inking capabilities, purchasing an accompanying pen completes that dual-screen experience. But the phone doesn't ship with a pen, supporting existing Surface inking accessories, like the Surface Pen, Surface Slim Pen, and the Surface Hub 2 Pen. However, Microsoft pitches the Surface Slim Pen as the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-pen-microsoft-surface-duo\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best pen for Surface Duo</a>, given its slimline silhouette that aids portability.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Add Pen And Touch</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">Microsoft Surface Slim Pen</h3>\n\n<p><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/field/image/2019/10/surface-slim-pen-cropped.jpg\"></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU79409YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fp%252Fsurface-slim-pen%252F8mn7mp9nqdlk&#38;token=8mGLnm63\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$112 at Microsoft</a>\n<a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUwpUdUnU79409YYr%26subId2%3Ddwp%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fmicrosoft-surface-slim-pen-black%252F6382264.p%253FskuId%253D6382264&#38;token=WfkinSK4\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">$118 at Best Buy</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Microsoft's sleek stylus joins the Surface Duo.</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Microsoft's latest stylus is a fantastic peripheral, sporting a slim design, wireless charging with an included cradle, and binding perfectly with the Surface Duo. It's the best way to experience mobile inking.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<p>The sleeker revamped pen debuted alongside the Surface Pro X in 2019, since appearing in Surface Duo marketing. The pen is more portable and better suited to the Duo design, leaving others feeling cumbersome in comparison. But the pen is just some of the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-surface-duo-accessories\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best Surface Duo accessories</a> out there, with more expected to hit the market later in 2020.</p>\n\n<h2>How to <em>demo</em> Surface Duo before launch</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-preorder-where-buy\" title=\"Surface Duo preorders: Price, release date, and where to buy\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-lady1.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>While the Microsoft Surface Duo doesn't launch until September 10, you can already experience a preview of the device both online and in-store. These opportunities provide a deeper dive into the dual-screen device, likely to answer the outstanding questions before placing your preorder.</p>\n\n<p>The best comes with by actually getting hands-on, with units now in <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-hands-demos-now-available-select-best-buy-locations\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">select physical Best Buy and AT&#38;T stores</a>. The demo allows for a feel of both hardware and software before launch, proving hugely valuable for a new form factor. We recommend calling your local store to check whether a device is on display. However, the Microsoft Store won't provide such experiences, given its <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-closing-all-physical-stores-part-strategic-change\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">recent decision to shutter all brick and mortar locations.</a></p>\n\n<p>If you have reservations about visiting your local store, online experiences are also on offer given current world events. The Microsoft Store now hosts <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D24542%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU79409YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.microsoft.com%252Fen-us%252Fstore%252Fworkshops-training-and-events%252Fsurface-duo&#38;token=K20cJjl1\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">regular live demo and Q&#38;A sessions</a>, where employees talk through the device, via a live video stream. You can also check <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-unboxing-watch-windows-centrals-daniel-rubino-go-hands\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">our pre-release unboxing</a> from Windows Central's executive editor Daniel Rubino, exploring the out-of-box experience for new buyers.</p>\n\n<h2>How much does Surface Duo <em>cost</em>?</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-preorder-where-buy\" title=\"Surface Duo preorders: Price, release date, and where to buy\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-peek.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>The Microsoft Surface Duo starts $1,399 with both unlocked and AT&#38;T-bound variants available for purchase. Preorders for the device come via the Microsoft Store, Best Buy, and AT&#38;T, before its U.S.-exclusive debut.</p>\n\n<p>The base Duo features 128GB onboard storage, under that $1,399 price tag. Microsoft also provides the option of a secondary 256GB model, priced at $1,499.</p>\n\n<p>You've likely noticed, the Microsoft Surface Duo isn't cheap. The device falls firmly within the premium smartphone bracket, outpacing rival flagships from Apple, Samsung, and more. It's easy to find an equally capable device in a traditional form factor for a lot less, including the new, top-of-the-line Samsung Galaxy Note20 Ultra at $1,299.</p>\n\n<p>But the Duo's premium price comes from its distinct design, pioneering an experimental dual-screen setup. The Samsung Galaxy Z Fold 2 comes in at $2,000, although with a price further inflated by that single, folding screen technology. But it's the expected cost for an early adopter of such devices.</p>\n\n<h2>What's in the <em>box</em> with Surface Duo?</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-preorder-where-buy\" title=\"Surface Duo preorders: Price, release date, and where to buy\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/surface-duo-press-in-box-accessories.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Microsoft Surface Duo ships with all the essentials, with the box containing the dual-screen device itself, a USB-C to USB-C cable, and the power adaptor. The package also has an included bumper case, which helps protect the edges of its glass screen and rear panels from scuffs and small drops.</p>\n\n<p>While the Surface Duo boasts inking support, Microsoft isn't shipping it with the required pen. Any Microsoft Surface pen will function, whether from an existing device, or purchased separately.</p>\n\n<h2 id=\"countries\">Which <em>countries</em> will Surface Duo be available in?</h2>\n\n<p>The Surface Duo launches exclusively in the U.S. for now, but Microsoft hasn't ruled out additional regions with time. The company's roots guaranteed the U.S. release, but its overseas absence is likely to disappoint more than a few budding buyers.</p>\n\n<p>We know Microsoft has additional markets on the roadmap, with past international documentation suggesting it's not exclusively U.S.-bound. The device's model number has popped up at both <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo-will-likely-ship-outside-us-based-new-certification\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Canada's UL LLC</a> and <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-surface-duo-passes-through-japanese-regulator-ahead-launch\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Japan's Ministry of Internal Affairs and Communications</a>, with launches in further regions expected.</p>\n\n<p>Launching a phone in new markets has its unique challenges, including consideration for popular cellular bands, and navigating local carriers. Expect more to come in the months ahead, as Surface Duo clears its U.S. arrival.</p>\n\n<h2 id=\"colors\">Which Surface Duo <em>colors</em> will be available?</h2>\n\n<p>While Microsoft's Surface family is famed for the brushed-platinum finish, other options such as burgundy, blue, gold, and black have emerged in time. However, with the Surface Duo, launch only offers a light-grey colorway dubbed \"Glacier.\"</p>\n\n<p>We know Microsoft has experimented with various dual-screen form factors over the years, including a black prototype in the hands of Microsoft Chief Product Officer, Panos Panay. But as with other Surface products, don't rule out the potential for additional colors with time — maybe for Surface Duo 2?</p>\n\n<h2 id=\"carriers\">Which <em>carriers</em> will Surface Duo come to?</h2>\n\n<p>Microsoft has confirmed the Surface Duo will support all major carriers, including AT&#38;T, T-Mobile, and Verizon Wireless in the United States. The unlocked model from Microsoft and Best Buy will likely work with your existing plan, while devices from AT&#38;T will be tied up with the service. The broad range of supported bands suggests that the Surface Duo will function overseas, allowing for a seamless transition into new markets.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category <p>Picking the right NAS for your home is primarily driven by the price of an enclosure. These servers can start relatively affordable, but the prices can quickly balloon into the thousands. The next most crucial factor is the number of drive bays. The higher the number, the more drives you could install, and the more capacity you can have for storing all your stuff.</p> \n    <p>Numerous vendors make NAS enclosures with some of the best models croming from Synology, QNAP, TerraMaster, and ASUSTOR. For most people, however, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Synology-Bay-DiskStation-DS220-Diskless/dp/B087ZCBWFH/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU47272YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Synology DiskStation DS220+</a> is the best choice overall. If it's not quite what you're looking for, the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Asustor-AS5304T-Inspired-Attached-Quad-Core/dp/B07PYJ2KNC?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU47272YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">ASUSTOR NIMBUSTOR 4 (AS5304T)</a> is an excellent second choice. For those who want to set up a Plex Media Server (PMS), the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07CDJ7NWR?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU47272YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">QNAP TVS-682-i3</a> is what you'll need.</p> \n    <p>You don't have to spend much to get a good NAS either. The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Synology-DS120j-DiskStation-Diskless-512MB/dp/B07ZKSLVT5/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU47272YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Synology DiskStation DS120j</a> and <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/TerraMaster-F2-221-Storage-Network-Diskless/dp/B07JHJHBDH/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU47272YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">TerraMaster F2-221</a> are fine examples of savings to be had without sacrificing too much on functionality, so long as you only plan on using these servers for file storage. An important fact to remember: Intel processors are generally more capable than ARM (basically non-Intel) CPUs.</p> \n    <p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Synology-Bay-DiskStation-DS220-Diskless/dp/B087ZCBWFH/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU47272YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-nas-home\" title=\"Best NAS for Home 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/08/synology-ds220-plus-render.jpg\" /></a></p> \n    <h2 id=\"bestoverall\">1. to purchase, you'll need to bear in mind a few factors. Do you intend to use the NAS for simply storing files? If so, what kind of files will you be storing? If you only plan on backing up several devices, you can get away with enclosures with but a few drive bays. If you want to replace your online cloud storage subscription service, you'll likely need four bays or more.</p> \n     <p>Price is essential with any purchase you make. No one wants to be spending more than they should on a product they may not get the most out of. We wouldn't want that either, which is why this collection of NAS exists to aid you in making the right decision. Whether or not you can upgrade the RAM inside a NAS, install an M.2 SSD to act as a cache and increase system performance, or hook up a 10Gb network line are all notable features.</p> \n     <p>The issue with going for a NAS enclosure that supports all the aforementioned, while coming with a powerful Intel CPU, is the price. The price doesn't look too bad now, right?</p> \n     <p>A NAS can remain relevant, especially if it has faster LAN ports, M.2 slots, plenty of drive bays, and one of the best processors you can buy right now. The former is simply a reflection of how much tech has been crammed into such a small package, but the weak CPU will be hard to live with if you expect decent performance for media streaming.</p> \n            <div class=\"rows left collection\"> \n             <h3 class=\"product reco-block\">Synology DiskStation DS419slim</h3> \n             <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-nas-home\" title=\"Best NAS for Home 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/synology-ds419slim-cropped-trans.png\" /></a></p> \n             <p>Synology's DiskStation DS419slim is an interesting NAS enclosure because it's not built for use at just your home. If you need portable storage that offers more than an external drive, this is the NAS for you.</p> \n             <p class=\"end\"><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Synology-Bay-2-5-DS419slim-Diskless/dp/B07T43VDMM/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU47272YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$330 at Amazon</a></p> \n            </div> \n            <hr> \n             <h2>What about all other NAS enclosures?</h2> \n             <p>There are so many NAS enclosures available; it's difficult to throw them all into a single collection. If, for some reason, you're not a fan of the DiskStation DS220+ from Synology, but desire a similar enclosure, you could pick a similar model from ASUSTOR, TerraMaster, or another vendor.</p> \n             <p>Regardless of what you plan on doing with the NAS enclosure, you can pick a model from any vendor and have a pleasant experience. Some operating systems are more refined (Synology) than others (TerraMaster), but largely they all operate similarly, which makes switching between vendors a breeze.</p> \n             <h2>What makes a good NAS enclosure?</h2> \n             <p>A good home NAS has a few drive bays (I'm talking between 1 and 4) with enough RAM to handle more than a single connection. 512MB of RAM can be enough, but if you intend to get everyone online in the home, you may want 1GB or more for better performance. For the CPU, it's all dependant on what you plan to use the NAS for.</p> \n             <p>There are so many NAS enclosures to choose from, which span different price points and specifications. You can find one that costs very little but gets you connected with smart storage, and another that costs far more and comes with more powerful hardware. Luckily, there's not a whole lot to a NAS enclosure, aside from these few specifications.</p> \n             <p>The speed of the Ethernet ports is of no concern since there's a strong possibility your LAN is restricted to just 1Gb. USB ports are handy if you plan on connecting accessories, external storage, or other devices, and eSATA is only handy if you plan on external using hard drives.</p> \n             <h2>How much performance do you need?</h2> \n             <p>Deciding on the processor of your NAS is a tricky one to make. ARM processors are pretty good and are used in a wide variety of hardware, including the smartphones we love to glue our eyes to each day. The thing is, they don't make for particularly good NAS servers if you aim to install Plex Media Server, run surveillance, and want to do more than a single task on the same NAS.</p> \n             <p>Intel processors are outstanding, much like their laptop- and desktop-class counterparts. Even Celeron and Atom processors are pretty good. Most modern Celeron CPUs in the latest models from vendors will even be able to handle 4K transcoding of movies on Plex. If you genuinely want to go all out with your NAS experience, try to pick one with an Intel Core series CPU.</p> \n             <p>Really, it all comes down to what you plan on doing with the NAS. If you will only store files and use it as a source for storing backups, an ARM processor is more than good enough. For anything else, it's best to go with an Intel CPU.</p> \n             <h2>What makes for a good Plex NAS?</h2> \n             <p>I've added an option in this collection for <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-nas-plex\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best NAS for Plex</a>, but what if you didn't have enough funds to cover the cost? Luckily for you, I also rounded up some fine NAS choices for running Plex Media Server. You don't need an enclosure with an Intel Core processor, so be sure to give that shortlist a look if you want something a little more affordable.</p> \n             <h2 class=\"no-amazon\">Credits — The team that worked on this guide</h2> \n             <p class=\"credit\"><img src=\"https://passport.mobilenations.com/avatars/000/001/025/1025269.jpg\" /></p> \n             <p class=\"end\"><strong>Rich Edmonds</strong> is a staff reviewer at Windows Central, which means he tests out more software and hardware than he cares to remember. Intel?</h2> \n    <p>Deciding on AMD or Intel for your processor (or already having one inside a rig you plan to upgrade) narrows the search for a new motherboard considerably. Intel motherboards come with Intel chipsets that only work with processors from the company, likewise with AMD. You cannot physically install an Intel CPU on an AMD motherboard or vice-versa. For most people, the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D44583%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU44470YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.newegg.com%252Fasus-rog-strix-x570-e-gaming%252Fp%252FN82E16813119111&amp;token=OGNQuOu3\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">ASUS ROG Strix X570-E Gaming</a> for AMD or <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/ASUS-ROG-Strix-Gaming-Motherboard/dp/B086QSH67R?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44470YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">ASUS ROG Strix Z490-E Gaming</a> for Intel will provide high stability and performance, allowing the rest of your PC to perform at their advertised potential. The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/ASUS-TUF-B550-PLUS-Motherboard-Addressable/dp/B088W57M4J/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44470YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">ASUS TUF Gaming B550-PLUS</a> or <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/MSI-Gaming-Motherboard-Socket-Mystic/dp/B0876HBFVC/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44470YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">MSI MPG Z490 Gaming Plus</a> will help you save some money, while the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/GIGABYTE-X399-AORUS-PRO-Destripador/dp/B07K8SJPMB/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44470YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">GIGABYTE X399 AORUS PRO</a> or <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/ASUS-ROG-XII-Motherboard-Bluetooth/dp/B086QT2Y86/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44470YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">ASUS ROG Maximus XII Hero Z490</a> are for those with deep pockets and high expectations.</p> \n    <p>Then you have specific chipsets from Intel and AMD that only work with certain processors. The X570 is best used for AMD Ryzen 3000 series processors. Intel's Z490 is good for 10th and 11th Gen processors. Take a gander at our full list of best motherboards to see which one best suits your PC build plan.</p> \n    <p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/ASUS-ROG-Motherboard-Lighting-Heatsinks/dp/B07SW8DQVL/?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44470YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-motherboards\" title=\"Best Motherboards 2020: For Gaming, AMD Ryzen, Intel\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/asus-rog-strix-x570-e-gaming-motherboard-cropped.jpg\" /></a></p> \n    <h2 id=\"bestamd\">1. ASUS ROG Strix X570-E Gaming: <em>Best Overall Motherboard for AMD PCs</em></h2> \n    <p><strong>Bottom line:</strong> Thanks to high-quality components, some serious heatsinks for the VRMs, and the best chipset from AMD make the ASUS ROG Strix X570-E Gaming one of the best motherboards available for AMD PCs in terms of value. It doesn't deliver all the features you'd find in enthusiast-grade boards, but this is about as good as you can get for a desktop motherboard.</p> \n    <p><strong>Socket:</strong> AM4 | it's also challenging to get it wrong, so long as you buy one that matches the CPU you intend to install. If we're choosing one that strikes a delicate balance between performance and price for AMD fans, it would be the <strong>ASUS ROG Strix X570-E Gaming</strong>. AMD's Ryzen generation of processors are dominating Intel, and the best motherboard for us from ASUS is a perfect match.</p> \n    <p>This isn't the <a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/CMQeEyOZF9Y/best-motherboards#enthusiastamd\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">most capable AMD motherboard</a>, but you likely won't require all the additional features that come with splashing out on the most premium motherboards around. The <strong>AM4</strong> platform is what has been used by AMD since Ryzen launched in 2017, and the <strong>X570</strong> is the latest high-end chipset from the company. This platform will support not only Ryzen 3000 processors that are out now but also 4000 series set to launch sometime in the future.</p> \n    <p>It's possible to install up to a <strong>maximum of 128GB RAM</strong>, using the four DIMM slots provided, though the likelihood of you requiring any more than 32GB is a stretch since only intensive workstations that handle huge files (video editing, for instance) need such large amounts.</p> \n    <p>The best part about the ROG Strix X570-E is the high-quality components used throughout. This is one of the more critical factors of choosing a motherboard, as well as a solid power delivery setup. Capacitors and other performance components should be part of a premium batch for enhanced reliability and better support for overclocking.</p> \n    <p>The rear port selection is pretty good for 2020 too. ASUS included DisplayPort and HDMI (for Ryzen CPUs with integrated graphics), Optical S/PDIF out, 2.5Gb LAN, Wi-Fi, seven USB 3.2 Gen 2 Type-A ports, as well as an additional USB 3.2 Gen 2 USB-C port. You can easily hook up all your favorite gaming accessories and then some.</p> \n    <p>You've also got RGB connectors, pump headers for water-cooling, two M.2 slots, plenty of SATA, and enough PCI slots to install all your favorite sound cards. It's not a budget motherboard, but you do get a lot for the money here. And because it's using AMD's latest chipset, you'll be able to take advantage of PCIe 4.0.</p> \n    <div class=\"rows left collection\"> \n     <h3 class=\"product reco-block\">ASUS ROG Strix X570-E Gaming</h3> \n     <p><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-motherboards\" title=\"Best Motherboards 2020: For Gaming, AMD Ryzen, Intel\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/asus-rog-strix-x570-e-gaming-motherboard-cropped.jpg\" /></a></p> \n     <p>Rocking a fantastic chipset, the ASUS ROG Strix X570-E is a fantastic motherboard for any Ryzen 3000 series CPU. You can install plenty of RAM and take advantage of the excellent stability and build quality.</p> \n     <p class=\"end\"><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fclick.linksynergy.com%2Fdeeplink%3Fid%3DkXQk6%252AivFEQ%26mid%3D44583%26u1%3DUUwpUdUnU44470YYr%26murl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.newegg.com%252Fasus-rog-strix-x570-e-gaming%252Fp%252FN82E16813119111&amp;token=OGNQuOu3\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><strong>2.</strong> ASUS ROG Strix Z490-E Gaming</a> (From $284)</li> \n      <li><a $495)</li> \n      <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/CMQeEyOZF9Y/best-motherboards#enthusiastintel\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><strong>4.</strong> ASUS ROG Maximus XII Hero Z490</a> (From $398)</li> \n      <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/CMQeEyOZF9Y/best-motherboards#itxamd\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><strong>5.</strong> Gigabyte X570 I AORUS Pro WIFI</a> (From $125)</li> \n      <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/CMQeEyOZF9Y/best-motherboards#itxintel\" $200)</li> \n      <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/wmexperts/~3/CMQeEyOZF9Y/best-motherboards#budgetintel\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><strong>8.</strong> MSI MPG Z490 Gaming Plus</a> (From $170)</li> \n     </ul> \n     <!--sectionbreak--> \n     <p>When looking at a motherboard to purchase, you'll want to consider a few factors. The first is which platform do you intend to use: Intel or AMD? Next is the chipset. These determine the features (and pricing) the motherboard can have, with the X570 and Z490 being the best choice for AMD and Intel, respectively. More budget-friendly chipsets like the B450 offer incredible value.</p> \n     <p>Speaking of value, price is a consideration worth making. It's recommended you spend a fair amount on a motherboard. You want to make sure you're getting high-quality components and decent cooling for the voltage regulator modules (VRM), which can get incredibly hot during operation, especially if you plan to push the system further through overclocking. Components like the VRMs come in all shapes and sizes, and it's down to the vendor to pick high-quality electronics for a more stable motherboard.</p> \n     <p>The processor you plan on using can also be of importance. Our enthusiast pick will be overkill for an AMD Ryzen 3 3100, for instance. On the flip side, you wouldn't want to install an AMD Ryzen 9 3900X on a B450 budget-friendly motherboard, since this would prevent you from overclocking the CPU, and the system may encounter stability issues with other components, like activating an XMP profile for RAM.</p> \n     <p>Motherboards can remain relevant for as long as your processor can keep up with what you require it to do. So long as you do not need to upgrade the CPU, it's usually safe to stick with your motherboard and install some faster, higher-capacity RAM, upgrade the storage, and get one of the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-graphics-cards\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">best graphics cards</a>. If you tend to only buy motherboards once in a blue moon and would prefer not to buy another for a good number of years, going with our best or enthusiast recommendations provide ample headroom for expansion in the future.</p> \n     <hr> \n      <p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/ASUS-ROG-Strix-Gaming-Motherboard/dp/B086QSH67R?tag=wpcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUwpUdUnU44470YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-motherboards\" title=\"Best Motherboards 2020: For Gaming, AMD Ryzen, Intel\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/07/asus-rog-strix-z490-cropped.jpg\" /></a></p> \n      <h2 id=\"bestintel\">2. By using a super-compact Mini-ITX case, it's possible to build a PC that takes up little more space than your favorite video game console.</p> \n         <p>As well as being physically smaller than ATX or micro-ATX motherboards, you retain a full PCIe slot with the <strong>Gigabyte X570 I AORUS Pro WIFI</strong>, can install <strong>two M.2 SSDs</strong>, throw in up to <strong>64GB of RAM</strong>, and the latest <strong>Ryzen 3000 CPUs</strong>. We've previously looked at motherboards for specific processors like the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-motherboards-for-amd-ryzen-9-3900x\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">AMD Ryzen 9 3900X</a> and the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-motherboards-intel-core-i7-10700k\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Intel Core i7-10700K</a>, as well as platforms like <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-motherboards-intel-cpus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Intel-only motherboards</a>.</p> \n             <p>Motherboards are available from different vendors, regardless of whether you go with Intel or AMD. For each of our picks, you could choose an alternative from another vendor and enjoy a similar experience. Usually speaking, motherboards tend to be more similar, though various factors like power delivery, component type, and features switched up to differentiate them.</p> \n             <hr> \n              <h2>Best Motherboards FAQ</h2> \n              <h3>How to choose the best motherboard</h3> \n              <p>Choosing the best motherboard for your <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/how-build-pc-ultimate-step-step-guide\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">PC build</a> largely depends on which processor you wish to use. Intel processors require motherboards with Intel sockets and chipsets, while AMD CPUs only work with respective AMD socket and chipset-touting boards. From there, you can look at price and chipset features, though so long as you spend a fair amount, you'll be buying an excellent motherboard.</p> \n              <p>The two best motherboards for either platform also allow for you to get much more from the processor than what's available from the factory, mostly with the included software handling everything for you. Other recommendations in our collection include solutions for enthusiasts, Mini-ITX builds, and those on a tighter budget. There really is a motherboard for almost everyone.</p> \n              <p>Usually, the more expensive the motherboard, the better the support for stable overclocking and the chance of high-quality components used.</p> \n              <h3>What you should look for in a new motherboard</h3> \n              <p>There are a few essential factors that should sway your decision making for a new motherboard. So long as you're not buying the lowest-priced boards, you'll generally be okay with the latest Intel and AMD processors. Here are a few things to bear in mind:</p> \n              <ul class=\"col2\"> \n               <li>Voltage regulator module (VRM) cooling.</li> \n               <li>Power delivery if you plan to overclock.</li> \n               <li>The rear port selection.</li> \n               <li>Form factor (ITX, microATX, ATX).</li> \n               <li>Choosing the right chipsets for AMD and Intel.</li> \n               <li>Matching said chipsets with the correct, supported CPU generation.</li> \n               <li>RAM support.</li> \n               <li>Features like M.2 slots.</li> \n              </ul> \n              <p>The VRMs and cooling them are both equally important. You want the power being delivered to the CPU to be clean and stable, especially if you plan on overclocking, which requires beefy VRMs for additional headroom. The power delivery with a high number of phases is also ideal, which is usually reserved for more expensive motherboards.</p> \n              <p>The rear port selection simply determines what ports will be available to you and your accessories. It's the least important factor in choosing a motherboard since most of the choices come with similar ports. Form factor determines the physical size of the motherboard, while chipsets from Intel and AMD are what help provided additional functionality.</p> \n              <p>It's important to match these to processors that are supported; the same goes for RAM. An Intel CPU won't work with an AMD motherboard and vice-versa. Some processors won't play well with slower or faster RAM, so be sure to double-check with Intel or AMD's website for additional details. Other features, like M.2 slots, are optional.</p> \n              <p>Our recommendations are a great place to start. We rounded up the very best for Intel and AMD processors, as well as options for Mini-ITX, budget, and enthusiast builds.</p> \n              <h2 class=\"no-amazon\">Credits — The team that worked on this guide</h2> \n              <p class=\"credit\"><img src=\"https://passport.mobilenations.com/avatars/000/001/025/1025269.jpg\" /></p> \n              <p class=\"end\"><strong>Rich Edmonds</strong> is a staff reviewer at Windows Central, which means he tests out more software and hardware than he cares to remember. If you hear him say, \"Sorry!\" it's only because he's Canadian.</p>\n             </hr>\n            </hr>\n           </hr>\n          </hr>\n         </hr>\n        </hr>\n       </hr>\n
